// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 0
śuklāmbaradharaṃ viṣṇuṃ śaśivarṇaṃ caturbhujam prasannavadanaṃ dhyāyet sarvavighnopaśāntaye

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 6
vyāsaprasādād vijñāya sarvaṃ vṛttāntam uttamam sainikānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ senayor ubhayos tadā khidyamānena manasā jagāma gajasāhvayam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 8
dhārtarāṣṭrān mṛtān sarvān manye saṃjaya saṃyuge

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 9
hataṃ śrutvā mama sutaḥ kim akārṣīc ca saṃjaya

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 10
saṃprāptāḥ kuravo yuddhe ke 'trātiṣṭhan paraṃtapāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 11
ko hi dauryodhane sainye pumān āsīn mahārathaḥ yaṃ prāpya sumahāyuddhe tan naḥ śaṃsa mahābhaye

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 15
jugupsamānāḥ paramaṃ kṣātraṃ karma viśāṃ pate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 23
karṇa karṇeti cakranduḥ śeṣā bhārata pārthivāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 26
lakṣmīr iva surais tyaktā śrutihīnā yathā dvijāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 42
cukruśuḥ sahitā yodhās tatra tatra mahābalāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 44
devān iva yathā viṣṇus trāyate mahato bhayāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 45
gāvalgaṇiṃ saṃjayaṃ tu śokavyākulalocanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 1, Verse 49
sa hi vai puruṣavyāghro loke saṃjaya kathyate ārtānāṃ bāndhavānāṃ ca krandatāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ parityajya raṇe prāṇāṃs tattrāṇārthaṃ ca śarma ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 2, Verse 3
saṃmṛjya divyaṃ dhanur ātatajyaṃ sa rāmadattaṃ ripusaṃghahantā bāṇāṃś ca kālānalatulyakalpān ullāḷayan vākyam idaṃ babhāṣe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 2, Verse 18
athābravīt sūtaputraḥ svasūtaṃ hantāsmy ahaṃ pāṇḍavasomakāṃś ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 3, Verse 1
utsādya cākhilām urvīṃ sarvakṣatrāntakaṃ gurum udyamyāpy atha vā meruṃ līlayākṣiptam ambhasi

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 3, Verse 8
**** **** śokamohapariplutaḥ padbhyām eva jagāmārto

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 3, Verse 18
nirdahantam anīkāni pravakṣyati janārdanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 3, Verse 22
so 'py adya nihataḥ śete śaraiḥ protaḥ śikhaṇḍinā jito yena raṇe rāmo bhavatā vīryaśālinā kṣatriyāntakaro ghoro devadānavapūjitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 4, Verse 3
mānahā bhava śatrūṇāṃ mitrāṇāṃ nandivardhanaḥ kauravāṇāṃ bhava gatir yathā viṣṇur divaukasām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 4, Verse 5
tathātibalavān rājā jarāsaṃdho 'dbhutopamaḥ samare samaraślāghī na tvayābhyadhiko raṇe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 4, Verse 6
utkalā mekalāḥ pauṇḍrāḥ kaliṅgāndhrāś ca saṃyuge niṣādāś ca trigartāś ca bāhlīkāś ca jitās tvayā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 4, Verse 8
kṣemaṃ vindati sarvatra śatruhāniṃ ca vindati

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 4, Verse 9
tathā kuru manuṣyendra yathā duryodhane jayam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 4, Verse 12
yathā ca kuravo yuddhe yodhayanti sma pāṇḍavān kṣatradharmārjitāṃl lokān avāpsyanti na saṃśayaḥ yudhyasva nirahaṃkāro balavīryavyapāśrayāt saṃjaya uvāca evam uktas tu bhīṣmeṇa yuddhāya kṛtaniścayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 4, Verse 13
atha tatra maheṣvāso vyādiśad rathino varān vāraṇāṃs tatprakāreṇa cakāra tadanantaram sādinaś ca padātāṃś ca yathāśāstraṃ bṛhaspatiḥ sthāpayām āsa tathā putrāṇāṃ te jayapriyaḥ tataḥ pakṣau prapakṣau ca vidhāya bharatarṣabha pakṣakoṭyāṃ punar dvābhyāṃ pakṣau dvābhyāṃ suhṛdvṛtaḥ evam etan mayā vyūhaṃ karṇena vihitaṃ purā prekṣaṇīyam amanyanta rājānaḥ kurubhiḥ saha nṛtyantam iva taṃ vyūhaṃ didhakṣantam ivāhitān kṛtaṃ bṛhaspatimataṃ matvā karṇena dhīmatā balaṃ vyūhaśarīrasya sārānīkaṃ parasparam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 4, Verse 14
hṛṣitāḥ kuravaḥ sarve duryodhanapurogamāḥ tam āgataṃ mahābāhuṃ sarvānīkapuraḥsaram

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 5, Verse 8
āhaveṣu viśeṣeṇa bhraṣṭanetreṣv ivāñjanam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 5, Verse 9
adaiśiko yathā sārthaḥ sarvaṃ pāpaṃ samarchati anāyakā tathā senā sarvān doṣān samarchati

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 5, Verse 27
sarveṣām eva lokānāṃ viśvasya ca yathā kṣayaḥ viśvotpattisthitilaye śreṣṭho nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 5, Verse 33
duryodhanaṃ tadā rājan droṇo vacanam abravīt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 5, Verse 35
pārṣataṃ tu raṇe rājan na haniṣye kathaṃ cana sa hi sṛṣṭo vadhārthāya mamaiva puruṣarṣabha yodhayiṣye tu sainyāni nāśayan sarvasomakān na ca māṃ pāṇḍavā yuddhe yodhayiṣyanti harṣitāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 5, Verse 37
svastivādaravaiś cānyaiḥ ślakṣṇaiḥ puṇyair manoramaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 5, Verse 40
prādurāsīn mahāśabdaḥ kṛte senāpatau dvije senāpatye mahātmānaṃ sarve saṃhṛṣṭamānasāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 6, Verse 18
dīpyan dṛśyeta hi tathā ketuḥ sarvatra dhīmataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 6, Verse 22
didhakṣantau raṇe kruddhau netrābhyām itaretaram niścarantau mahāvīryau dhunvānau dhanuṣī dṛḍhau samucchritapatākena dhvajena rathināṃ varaḥ ācāryaḥ kurupāṇḍūnāṃ saṃgrāmaśirasi sthitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 7, Verse 25
śreṇīkṛtāḥ saṃyati moghavegā dvīpe nadīnām iva kāśarohāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 7, Verse 29
sa tu kṛtvā mahatkarma droṇaḥ parabalārdanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 7, Verse 36
vicitrajāmbūnadabhūṣitadhvajaṃ mahārathaṃ rukmarathaṃ nipātitam niśamya kaś cid dhi na harṣam eyivān ṛte mṛdhe drupadasutāt sasṛñjayāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 8, Verse 9
daivam eva paraṃ manye na sunītaṃ na pauruṣam madīyo nāyako yatra guṇaśreṣṭho hataḥ paraiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 8, Verse 14
guṇānāṃ sarvayodhānāṃ sthitir āsīn mahādyutiḥ yaṃ mṛtyur vaśagas tiṣṭhet sa kathaṃ mṛtyunā hataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 8, Verse 19
taṃ tu rukmarathaṃ dṛṣṭvā vidravanti sma śatravaḥ divyam astraṃ vikurvāṇaṃ saṃgatāḥ sarvataḥ pare

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 8, Verse 26
utsṛjya sarvasainyāni droṇam evābhidudruve

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 8, Verse 29
dṛptānāṃ pratiṣeddhā ca cakṣur āsīd acakṣuṣām amarṣī cāvalipteṣu dhārmikeṣu ca dhārmikaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 8, Verse 33
vā kathaṃ nihataḥ pāpai raṇe brāhmaṇapuṃgavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 8, Verse 34
adīnaṃ puruṣavyāghraṃ hrīmantam aparājitam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 8, Verse 35
brahmakalpo 'bhavad brāhme kṣātre nārāyaṇopamaḥ brahmakṣatre ca yasyāstāṃ vaśe sthāṇor ivākhile sarvān hi māmakān yuddhe sahāśvarathakuñjarān yudhiṣṭhirasya tapasā hatān manyāmahe kurūn

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 8, Verse 37
yaḥ sa devān sagandharvān sayakṣoragarākṣasān jetum utsahate droṇaḥ sa kathaṃ nihataḥ paraiḥ na sa pṛṣṭham ares trāsād raṇe śauryāt pradarśayet parām apy āpadaṃ prāpya sa kathaṃ nihataḥ paraiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 8, Verse 38
kaccin nainaṃ bhayāt kṣudrāḥ pārthebhyaḥ pradadū raṇe goptṛbhis taiḥ samutsṛṣṭaḥ kaccin naiṣa parair hataḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ hi paśyāmi nighnantam iva brāhmaṇam vāryamāṇaṃ raṇe tāta drauṇināmitatejasā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 8, Verse 39
kṣaṇam ekam ahaṃ sūta na śakṣyāmīti jalpitum

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 9, Verse 12
yaḥ karoti mahatkarma śatrūṇāṃ vai mahābalaḥ mahākāyo mahotsāho nāgāyutasamo bale

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 9, Verse 17
gadāsividyutkalilaḥ śātravāṇāṃ bhayaṃkaraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 9, Verse 18
yadāyāt katham āsīd vas tadā pārthaṃ samīkṣya ha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 9, Verse 20
ko hi śakto raṇe jetuṃ mānavaḥ pārtham īkṣitum

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 9, Verse 26
taṃ rathānāṃ varaṃ vīraṃ sadā yuddheṣu durmadam nakulaṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭhaṃ ke vīrāḥ paryavārayan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 9, Verse 27
amoghabāṇaḥ siddheṣuḥ śatrubhir yudhi durjayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 9, Verse 28
ārāvaṃ tumulaṃ kurvan vyathayan bhairavaṃ raṇe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 9, Verse 32
dhanaṃjayopadeśena śreṣṭham iṣvastrakarmaṇi

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 9, Verse 34
yasmin nityāni santi sma vīre satyaparākrame

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 9, Verse 62
visṛṣṭā dakṣiṇā yasya gaṅgājalam avārayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 10, Verse 2
śakaṭaṃ pūtanāṃ hatvā bhagnau ca yamalārjunau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 10, Verse 5
pūtanāṃ śakuniṃ hatvā keśinaṃ caiva vājinam ṛṣabhaṃ dhenukaṃ caiva ariṣṭaṃ ca mahābalam vṛkaṃ hatvā mahābāhuṃ dhṛtvā govardhanaṃ girim cāṇūraṃ muṣṭikaṃ caiva raṅgamadhye nihatya ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 10, Verse 23
govardhanasyoddharaṇe jñātvā vai samasajjata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 10, Verse 31
eka eva dvidhā bhūto dṛśyate mānuṣair bhuvi

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 10, Verse 32
pitṝṇām api yaḥ pūrvo vedeṣu paripaṭhyate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 10, Verse 38
sarveṣv api ca lokeṣu bībhatsur aparājitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 11, Verse 1
śuśrūṣasva sthiro bhūtvā śaṃsato mama bhārata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 11, Verse 3
anurūpaṃ phalaṃ tasya karmaṇo labhyatāṃ tvayā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 11, Verse 6
iccheyaṃ vai mahātmānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram bhrātṝṇāṃ paśyatām eva jīvagrāheṇa me dvija prīṇāmy anena kāryeṇa sasuhṛjjanabāndhavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 11, Verse 16
yadi sarve haniṣyante pāṇḍavāḥ sasutā mṛdhe tataḥ kṛtsnaṃ vaśe kṛtvā niḥśeṣaṃ nṛpamaṇḍalam sasāgaravanāṃ sphītāṃ vijitya vasudhām imām viṣṇur dāsyati kṛṣṇāyai kuntyai vā puruṣottamaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 11, Verse 17
tasmiñ jīvati cānīte hy upāyair bahubhiḥ kṛtaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 11, Verse 21
sthite pārthe dharmarājo naiva śakyo mayā raṇe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 11, Verse 29
evam ukte tadā tasmin yuddhe devāsuropame

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 11, Verse 31
skandhāvāreṣu sarveṣu yathāsthāneṣu māriṣa

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 12, Verse 12
anyac ca brūyāṃ rājendra pratijñāṃ mama nityadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 10
keśaśaivālasaṃyuktāṃ māṃsāsṛkkardamāruṇām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 14
śarīraśatasaṃbādhāṃ gṛdhrakaṅkaniṣevitām mahārathasahasrāṇi nayantīṃ yamasādanam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 16
nadīṃ prāsyandayan droṇaḥ keśaśaivalaśāḍvalām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 17
uvāha śataśo rājan pitṛlokāya vāhinīm

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 22
bhittvā ca śaravarṣeṇa śakuniṃ pratyavārayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 25
tayos tatra mahārāja bāṇavarṣaiḥ prakāśitam khadyotair iva cākāśaṃ pradoṣe puruṣarṣabha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 27
cakre taṃ sarvasainyāni prahṛṣṭāny abhyapūjayan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 28
hatāśvāt sa rathād rājan gṛhya carma mahābalaḥ abhyayād bhīmasenaṃ tu matto mattam iva dvipam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 30
ciccheda samare yattaḥ sa ca yuddhād upāramat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 38
bhagadattas tu rājānaṃ drupadaṃ nataparvabhiḥ saniyantṛdhvajarathaṃ vivyādha puruṣarṣabhaḥ drupadas tu tataḥ kruddho bhagadattaṃ mahāratham ājaghānorasi kṣipraṃ śareṇānataparvaṇā yuddhaṃ yodhavarau loke saumadattiśikhaṇḍinau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 40
chādayām āsa nārācais tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 43
tayos tu yuddham abhavat parasparavadhaiṣiṇau yudhiṣṭhiraḥ svayaṃ rājā duryodhanam ayodhayat tau putrau tava durdharṣau yuyudhāte parasparam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 49
tasya saṃdhitam ājñāya sāyakaṃ ghoradarśanam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 60
dudhāva sahasā khaḍgaṃ carma cātirathaḥ punaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 13, Verse 78
parivavruḥ sma te sarve pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ harṣayantaś ca saubhadraṃ roṣayantaḥ sutāṃś ca te

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 14, Verse 1
na hi devāsuraṃ yuddham īdṛgrūpaṃ bhaved iti cintayāmi ca yuddhāni śrutvā ghorāṇi saṃjaya

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 14, Verse 13
sāgnidīptā mahāraudrā gadā sā śuśubhe tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 14, Verse 15
kopatāmrekṣaṇau vīrau śatrusaṃghavimardanau mahāmātrau mahotsāhau gadāyuddhaviśāradau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 14, Verse 20
bhīmarūpā mahāvegā gadā śalyaṃ raṇe 'nudat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 14, Verse 21
punaḥ śalyena bhīmasya gadāgrād gadayā hatāt saṃgharṣaṇād utthito 'gnir dīpayām āsa medinīm punaś ca bhīmasenena śalyasya mahatī gadā tāḍitā sahasā rājan visasarjātha pāvakam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 14, Verse 37
atha maḍḍukabherimahāmurajāḥ paṇavānakadundubhijharjharibhiḥ vinadanti bhṛśaṃ saha śaṅkharavair vividhaiś ca narottama siṃharavaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 15, Verse 15
prajānāṃ saṃkṣaye ghore yathā sūryodayo bhavet śūrāṇām udayas tadvat sa āsīt puruṣarṣabha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 15, Verse 25
bāṇair nivārayām āsa paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvinām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 15, Verse 31
taṃ vijitya mahātejā bhāradvājo mahāmanāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 15, Verse 40
asmin muhūrte droṇas tu pāṇḍavaṃ gṛhya harṣitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 15, Verse 41
mā bhaiṣīr iti saṃvārya śarair droṇam avārayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 16, Verse 9
kṣobhayitvā balaṃ teṣāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 16, Verse 20
maladāś ca karūśāś ca daradāś ca mahārathāḥ taṅkaṇāś ca parādāś ca yugapatte samāgatāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 16, Verse 26
dvijamukhyaiḥ samuditaiḥ kṛtasvasty ayanāśiṣaḥ muditāś ca prahṛṣṭāś ca jalaṃ saṃspṛśya nirmalam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 16, Verse 34
satyam ākramatāṃ ye ca pratyādityaṃ pramehatām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 16, Verse 41
na hy arjuno raṇe rājan mithyā kiṃ cit pravakṣyati hatāṃs traigartakān paśya mā sma te kaśmalaṃ bhavet

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 16, Verse 44
sarvathā na nivarteyam āhūto 'haṃ paraṃtapa trigarto bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ sa mām āhvayate bhṛśam tavāpi tu raṇe rakṣā vihitā me janādhipa nirapekṣo gamiṣyāmi vadhāyaiṣāṃ durātmanām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 16, Verse 48
grahaṇe dharmarājasya kṛtotsāhaṃ mahāmṛdhe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 16, Verse 49
vegena śaṅkhān āpūrya harṣayukte mahāsvane

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 17, Verse 2
atīva saṃprahṛṣṭās te hy upalakṣya dhanaṃjayam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 17, Verse 6
mayā hatā hi saṃgrāme lokān prāpsyanti puṣkalān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 17, Verse 9
sā senā bharataśreṣṭha niśceṣṭā śuśubhe tadā citrapaṭṭe yathā nyastā kuśalaiḥ śilpibhir naraiḥ svanena tena sainyānāṃ divam āvṛṇvatā tadā sasvanā pṛthivī sarvā tathaiva ca mahodadhiḥ vyūḍhānīkais tu taiḥ sarvaiḥ pṛthivyāṃ samarārṇave svanena sarvasainyānāṃ karṇās tu badhirīkṛtāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 17, Verse 10
tato vyupāramac chabdaḥ prahṛṣṭās te tato 'bhavan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 17, Verse 22
jahāra pārthaḥ sainyeṣu sahasre dve ca yodhinām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 17, Verse 23
bhūyiṣṭhaṃ pratiruddhās te hatair yodhair yaśasvinaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 18, Verse 4
evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ bībhatsuṃ keśavaḥ śatruvāhinīm

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 18, Verse 13
anyonyaṃ samare jaghnus tāvakā bharatarṣabha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 18, Verse 14
rudhirotpīḍanās te tu rudhireṇa samukṣitāḥ candanasya raseneva vyabhrājanta raṇājire tataḥ prahasya bībhatsur vyākṣipad gāṇḍivaṃ bhṛśam nyahanat tāñ śarais tīkṣṇais tamaḥ sūrya ivāṃśubhiḥ hatāvaśiṣṭās te bhūyaḥ parivārya dhanaṃjayam sāśvadhvajarathaṃ cakrur adṛśyaṃ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 19, Verse 26
sa hi jāto mahāraudro droṇasya nidhanaṃ prati martyadharmatayā tasmād bhāradvājo vyamuhyata nāśakat taṃ tataḥ kaś cid anīke prativīkṣitum tataḥ kirann iṣūṃs tīkṣṇān drupadasya varūthinīm bhāradvājo yayau tūrṇaṃ pārṣataṃ varjayan yudhi drupadasya mahat sainyaṃ vārayām āsa brāhmaṇaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 19, Verse 31
abhavat tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ parasparavadhaiṣiṇoḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 19, Verse 33
naiva khaṃ na diśo bhūmir babhāse na ca bhāskaraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 19, Verse 52
gajair gātravaraiḥ kṣuṇṇā viṣāṇaś ca nipātitāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 20, Verse 4
tato droṇaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ satyajit satyavikramaḥ avidhyan niśitāgraiś ca paramāstraṃ vidarśayan tato 'sya sāratheḥ pañca śarān sarpaviṣopamān amuñcad antakaprakhyān saṃmumohāsya sārathiḥ athāsya sahasāvidhyad dhayān daśabhir āśugaiḥ daśabhir daśabhiḥ kruddha ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī maṇḍalaṃ tu samāvṛtya vyacarat pṛtanāmukhe dhvajaṃ ciccheda ca kruddho droṇasyāmitrakarśanaḥ droṇas tu tat samālakṣya caritaṃ tasya saṃyuge manasā cintayām āsa prāptakālam ariṃdamaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 20, Verse 5
ācāryas tasya vai cāpaṃ ciccheda tribhir āśugaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 20, Verse 15
avākirac charais tūrṇaṃ bhāradvājaṃ samantataḥ hayeṣu ca viṣakteṣu vimukho 'bhavad āhave

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 20, Verse 16
vegena mahatāmṛdnād vāto drumam ivocchritam tataḥ pāñcālaputrasya yuddhe satyajitas tathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 20, Verse 21
krūrāya karmaṇe yuktaṃ cikīrṣuḥ karma duṣkaram avākirac charaśatair bhāradvājaṃ samantataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 20, Verse 29
śobhamānāṃ dhvaje cāsya vedīm adrākṣma bhārata himavacchikharākārāṃ carataḥ saṃyuge bhṛśam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 20, Verse 38
te droṇaṃ sahitāḥ śūrāḥ sarvataḥ paryavārayan gabhastibhir ivādityaṃ tapantaṃ bhuvane yathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 20, Verse 39
śikhaṇḍī tu tato droṇaṃ pañcabhir nataparvabhiḥ kṣatravarmā ca viṃśatyā vasudānaś ca pañcabhiḥ uttamaujās tribhir bāṇaiḥ kṣatradevaś ca saptabhiḥ sātyakiś ca śatenājau yudhāmanyus tathāṣṭabhiḥ yudhiṣṭhiro dvādaśabhir droṇaṃ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca daśabhiś cekitānas tribhiḥ śaraiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 20, Verse 47
taṃ hatvā vibabhau droṇaḥ kurubhiḥ parivāritaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 20, Verse 52
vārdhakṣemis tu vārṣṇeyo droṇaṃ viddhvā śarottamaiḥ navabhiś cāvanīpālaḥ punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ citrasenas tato droṇaṃ pāñcālas tv ardayac charaiḥ punar vivyādha saṃkruddhaḥ senābinduś ca pañcabhiḥ suvarmā pañcabhiś caiva dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pañcabhiḥ śikhaṇḍī navabhir bāṇaiś cekitānaś ca pañcabhiḥ sātyakiś ca catuḥṣaṣṭyā rājan vivyādha sāyakaiḥ sucitro daśabhir bāṇair droṇaṃ viddhvānadad balī taṃ droṇaḥ samare rājañ śaravarṣair avākirat apātayat tato droṇaḥ sucitraṃ sahasārathim sāśvaś ca samare rājan hato vai prāpatat kṣitau pātyamāno mahārāja babhau jyotir ivāmbarāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 21, Verse 24
eṣa cāpi mahābāhur himavān iva susthiraḥ vadhiṣyati mahārāja gadayā bhīmavegayā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 21, Verse 25
hrīmantaḥ śatrumaraṇe nipuṇāḥ puṇyalakṣaṇāḥ bahavaḥ pārthivā rājaṃs teṣāṃ vaśagatā raṇe māvamaṃsthāḥ pāṇḍavāṃs tvaṃ nārāyaṇapurogamān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 22, Verse 1
tān ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi vistareṇa pṛthak pṛthak dūyate me manas tāta droṇaṃ prati paraṃtapa śrutvā bhīṣmasya nidhanaṃ tadvad etad bhaviṣyati

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 22, Verse 2
sāraṅgaiś ca yudhāmanyur uhyamāno hayottamaiḥ paryavartata durdharṣaḥ kruddho droṇarathaṃ prati pārāvatasavarṇais tu hemabhāṇḍair mahājavaiḥ pāñcālarājasya suto dhṛṣṭadyumno 'bhyavartata pitaraṃ tu pariprepsuḥ kṣatradharmā yatavrataḥ siddhiṃ cāsya parāṃ kāṃkṣañ śoṇākṣaḥ saṃnyavartata padmapatranibhaiś cāśvair mallikākṣair alaṃkṛtaiḥ śikhaṇḍī kṣatradevaś ca svayaṃ pratvarayan yayau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 22, Verse 4
dantavarṇās tu rājānaṃ kālavālā yudhiṣṭhiram durdharṣāyābhisaṃdhāya kruddhaṃ kruddhāya bhārata tathā tittirikalmāṣā hayā vātasamā jave avahaṃs tumule yuddhe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 22, Verse 18
rukmabhāṇḍapraticchannāḥ kauśeyasadṛśā hayāḥ kṣamāvanto 'vahan saṃkhye senābindum araṭṭajāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 22, Verse 20
yuvānam avahan yuddhe yantuḥ preṣyakarāḥ hayāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 22, Verse 22
sahasrasomapratimā hayāḥ kanakabhūṣaṇāḥ vīraṃ tam avahan yuddhe heṣamāṇāḥ samantataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 22, Verse 46
rāsabhāruṇavarṇābhāḥ pṛṣṭhato mūṣakaprabhāḥ valganta iva saṃyattā vyāghradantam udāvahan harayaḥ kālakāś citrāś citramālyavibhūṣitāḥ sudhanvānaṃ naravyāghra pāñcālyaṃ samudāvahan indrāśanisamasparśā indragopakasaṃnibhāḥ kośaiś citrāntarāś citrāś citrāyudham udāvahan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 22, Verse 58
keśavena hate saṃkhye pitary atha narādhipe bhinne kapāṭe pāṇḍyānāṃ vidruteṣu ca bandhuṣu bhīṣmād avāpya cāstrāṇi droṇād rāmāt kṛpāt tathā astraiḥ samatvaṃ saṃprāpya rukmikarṇārjunācyutaiḥ iyeṣa dvārakāṃ hantuṃ kṛtsnāṃ jetuṃ ca medinīm nivāritas tataḥ prājñaiḥ suhṛdbhir hitakāmyayā vairānubandham utsṛjya svarājyam anuśāsti yaḥ sasāgaradhvajaḥ pāṇḍyaś candraraśminibhair hayaiḥ vaiḍūryajālasaṃchannair vīryadraviṇam āśritaḥ divyaṃ visphārayaṃś cāpaṃ droṇam abhyapatad balī

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 22, Verse 60
nānādhvajapatākena nānākavacavājinā gato yudhiṣṭhiraṃ bhaktyā tyaktvā sarvasvam īhitam lohitākṣaṃ mahābāhuṃ bṛhantaṃ taṃ varadhvajam mahāsattvā mahākāyā sauvarṇe syandane sthitam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 23, Verse 16
tau droṇabhīṣmau nihitau kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 23, Verse 19
kathaṃ ca vo manas tāta saṃnivṛtteṣv avartata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 24, Verse 4
evam uktvā svayaṃ bhīmam abhyayāt tanayas tava krūraṃ dṛṣṭvā tu te putraṃ bhīmaseno 'bhyavartata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 24, Verse 14
duḥśāsanas tu saṃyāntaṃ droṇāya nakulaṃ yudhi savyadakṣiṇam asyantaṃ śūraḥ śūraṃ nyavārayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 24, Verse 25
sālvo bhīmarathaḥ śūraṃ śrutasenaṃ mahāhave droṇāyābhimukhaṃ yāntaṃ śaraugheṇa nyavārayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 24, Verse 27
tam ārjuniḥ śaraiś cakre pitṛvyaṃ jarjarac chavim śaraiś ca draupadīputraṃ citrasenaḥ samāvṛṇot kirantaṃ śarajālāni prabhinnam iva kuṃjaram śrutakarmāṇam āyāntaṃ dauḥśāsanir avāyat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 24, Verse 28
mahārathaṃ tu saubhadraṃ sarvayuddhaviśāradam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 24, Verse 31
ārjuniṃ śrutakīrtiṃ ca draupadeyaṃ mahāratham droṇāyābhimukhaṃ yāntaṃ dauḥśāsanir avārayat tasya kṛṣṇasamaḥ kārṣṇis tribhir bhallaiḥ susaṃśitaiḥ dhanur dhvajaṃ ca sūtaṃ ca chittvā droṇāntikaṃ yayau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 24, Verse 33
tato 'bhimanyuḥ karmāṇi kurvantaṃ citrayodhinam ārjuniḥ kṛtinaṃ śūraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ samayodhayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 24, Verse 37
aṅgadaṃ pañcabhir bāṇair avidhyat sa paraṃtapaḥ aṅgado daśabhir bāṇaiḥ punar enam avākirat tataḥ samabhavad yuddham anyonyam itaretaram vīrāṇāṃ jayakāṅkṣāṇām atīva balapauruṣāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 24, Verse 44
bṛhaddhanur bṛhac caiva jayamitro jayas tathā dhṛṣṭadyumnasutān vīrān putrās te samavārayan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 24, Verse 54
pārtham indram ivāyāntaṃ droṇaṃ prati nijaghnuṣam samārcchat sāyakaughena svayaṃ rājā nyavārayat sa nṛpaṃ sāśvayantāram arātighnam arātihā amṛdnāt taṃ pṛṣatkena duryodhanam ariṃdamam sa jyāṃ mṛdnatpṛṣatkena spṛṣṭvā vṛkṣam ivāśaniḥ vīro vismāpayan yuddhe droṇāyābhimukho 'vrajat alambusas tu saṃkruddho ghaṭotkacam avārayat vṛkarkṣayukte tiṣṭhantaṃ rathe vīro vareṣubhiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 24, Verse 58
bhāradvājas tu senānyaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ mahāratham tam eva rājan saṃpaśyann atikramya tathā bahūn mahatā śarajālena kirantaṃ śatruvāhinīm avārayan mahārāja sāmātyaṃ sapadānugam tathānye pārthivā rājan bahutvān nānukīrtitāḥ samasajjanta te sarve yathāyogaṃ yathābalam hayair hayāḥ samājagmuḥ kuñjarair eva kuñjarāḥ padātayaḥ padātaiś ca rathair eva ratharṣabhāḥ akurvann āryakarmāṇi tatra te puruṣarṣabhāḥ kulavīryānurūpāṇi saṃsṛṣṭāś ca parasparam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 5
tatra yuddhāny adṛśyanta pradṛptāni bahūni ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 20
tadanvayena nāgena bhīmasenam upādravat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 21
vṛkodararathaṃ sāśvam aviśeṣam acūrṇayat padbhyāṃ bhīmo 'py atho dhāvaṃs tasya gātreṣv alīyata jānann añjalikāvedhaṃ nāpākrāmata pāṇḍavaḥ gātrābhyantarago bhūtvā kareṇātāḍayan muhuḥ lālayām āsa taṃ nāgaṃ vadhākāṅkṣiṇam avyayam kulālacakravan nāgas tadā tūrṇam athābhramat nāgāyutabalaḥ śrīmān kālayāno vṛkodaram bhīmo 'pi niṣkramya tataḥ supratīkāgrato 'bhavat bhīmaṃ kareṇāvanamya jānubhyām abhyapātayat grīvāyāṃ veṣṭayitvainaṃ sa gajo hantum aihata karaveṣṭaṃ bhīmaseno bhramaṃ dattvā vyamocayat punar gātrāṇi nāgasya praviveśa vṛkodaraḥ yāvat pratigajāyātaṃ svabalastham avaikṣata bhīmo 'pi nāgagātrebhyo viniḥsṛtyāpayāj javāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 24
bhīmo 'pi dorbhyāṃ nāgendraṃ nipīḍyāmocayad balī

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 30
prāgjyotiṣānādhipater gatvā nā[ga]m abodhayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 31
tato yudhiṣṭhiro dṛṣṭvā daśārṇādhipatiṃ hatam mahatā rathavaṃśena prāgjyotiṣam abhidravat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 35
so 'tividdho balavatā satyakena viśāṃ pate vyavartata paritrāsān maṇḍalāni śarārditaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 49
yuyutsus tu rathād rājann apākrāmat tvarānvitaḥ tataḥ pāṇḍavayodhās te nāgarājaṃ śarair drutam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 50
sa bhīmenātha bahudhā dantābhyām avapīḍayan mokṣito yuddhaśauṇḍena nāgāyutabalo gajaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 51
cekitānaś catuḥṣaṣṭyā sottarāyudhikaṃ punaḥ pratyavidhyac charaiḥ sarvān bhagadattas tribhis tribhiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 55
abhidhāveti kaunteyaṃ saṃcodayad ivārjunam samucchrito bhṛśārtāyā senāyā subhujo yathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 25, Verse 57
samantatas tatra janādhipeśvara

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 26, Verse 6
siṃhanādaṃ mahat kṛtvā dhanurbāṇaravaiḥ saha vidrāvyamāṇaṃ saṃpaśya hatabhūyiṣṭhanāyakam dṛṣṭvā vinadya sahasā mama senāṃ pramṛdnati

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 26, Verse 19
tatas tena śaraugheṇa mahatā samavāstṛtaḥ nāśakan nāma bībhatsur amitrān pratibādhitum

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 26, Verse 20
tato janārdanaḥ pārthaṃ pratyuvāca hasann iva vajram astraṃ tu saṃdhāya jahi saṃśaptakān iha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 26, Verse 28
karmaitat pārtha śakreṇa yamena dhanadena ca duṣkaraṃ samare yat te kṛtam adyeti me matiḥ yugapac caiva saṃgrāme śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ patitā eva me dṛṣṭāḥ saṃśaptakamahārathāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 27, Verse 25
vavarṣa śaravarṣaṃ tu punar eva dhanaṃjayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 8
**** **** tad vyaśīryata bhūtale viśīrṇavarmā sa gajaḥ śaraiḥ subhṛśam arditaḥ babhau śirasi mātaṃgo

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 14
tau vidhyamānau nārācair bhagadattena bhārata jagmatur naiva saṃmohaṃ cukṣubhāte na cācyutau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 16
tad astram udyataṃ dṛṣṭvā vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān arjunaḥ pṛṣṭhataṃ kṛtvā pratijagrāha vīryavān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 18
padmakośavicitrā ca sarvartukusumākulā jvalanārkenduvarṇāḍhyā tārakojjvalapāvakā tayā padmābhiśobhinyā vāyukampitalolayā śobhate 'bhyadhikaṃ śauriratasīpuṣpasaṃnibhaḥ keśavaḥ keśimathanaḥ śārṅgadhanvārimardanaḥ sandhyābhrair iva saṃchannaḥ prāvṛṭkāle nagottamaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 19
idam astram avasthāpya prāptaṃ māṃ devakīsuta kimarthaṃ puruṣavyāghra svayaṃ pratigṛhītavān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 22
tad etan narakasyāsīd astraṃ sarvāhitāntakam tasmāt prāgjyotiṣaṃ prāptaṃ sarvaśastravighātanam nāsyāvadhyo 'sti loke 'smin mad anyaḥ kaś cid arjuna tasmān mayā kṛtaṃ hy etan mā te 'bhūd buddhir anyathā anunīya tu dāśārhaḥ pāṇḍavaṃ tvarito 'bravīt jahi prāgjyotiṣaṃ kṣipraṃ vākyaśeṣaṃ ca me śṛṇu

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 32
vyajāyata dharā devī putraṃ putraśatāvaram

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 33
tad astraṃ devagandharvayakṣapannagarākṣasān sarvān samāgatān hanyāt kiṃ punas tvāṃ dhanaṃjaya bhogināṃ caiva durdharṣaṃ mayā dattaṃ surāsuraiḥ jahi prāgjyotiṣaṃ pārtha purā sarvān hinasti saḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 35
avadhyo 'yaṃ mahāstreṇa bhagadattaḥ surāsuraiḥ yathāhaṃ narakaṃ lokahitārtham ahanaṃ purā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 36
ghaṇṭāṃ kāñcanasaṃchannāṃ viśvakarmavinirmitām kāñcanaśṛṅkhalānaddhāṃ savyāṃ ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ sā hatā śaraghātena vajraniṣpeṣasaṃnibhā papāta dūrapātena candrabimbasamujjvalā dakṣiṇāpi hatā rājan ghaṇṭā bāṇaiḥ kirīṭinaḥ papāta dūram adhvānaṃ gatvā sūrya iva kṣitau bhagadattena nirmuktaḥ supratīko 'pi vegataḥ hanumān sūryabimbasya grasanārtham ivodyataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 37
tataḥ saṃdhāya viśikhaṃ dīpyamānam ivānalam avidhyad arjuno nāgaṃ kumbhayor antare bhṛśam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 38
madhye vidīrṇas tasthau sa prāsyandata punaḥ punaḥ syandamānaṃ tato nāgaṃ caraṇābhyām anodayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 39
tamomayaṃ jagan mene bhagadattaḥ pratāpavān devavākyāt praciccheda śareṇa bhṛśam arjunaḥ chinnamātreṃ 'śuke tasmin ruddhanetro babhūva saḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 28, Verse 40
bibheda sakalo deho dvidhābhūto babhūva ha rājñā balavatā tena jānubhyāṃ dhārito raṇe arjunaṃ prati yuddhe na cirakālaṃ dadhāra saḥ evaṃ yuddhaṃ tadā tena rājñā tena durātmanā kirīṭī cārdhabimbena śareṇānataparvaṇā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 29, Verse 1
pūrvadaityaṃ mahāvīraṃ bhagadattaṃ mahābalam kṛṣṇau daśārhabībhatsū jaghnatur yudhi durjayam nāgāyutabalaprāṇaṃ śūram āhavaśobhinam supratīko 'pi balavān nāgāyutasamo balī vaiṣṇavāstreṇa saṃyukto aṃkuśena ca vīryavān trīṇi tejāṃsi tatraiva tretāgnir iva cādhvare bhagadattaṃ raṇe śūraṃ nihanyāt ko 'rjunaṃ vinā arjuno 'pi mahāvīryo hatvā pitṛsakhaṃ raṇe kṣatradharmaṃ vicintyājau dhig dhig ity eva cābravīt tam ādityasamaṃ kāntyā bhūmau nipatitaṃ divaḥ prasamīkṣya tadā pārtho reṇunā tv avaguṇṭhitam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 29, Verse 23
tat tamo bhairavaṃ ghoraṃ bhayakartṛ mahāhave

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 29, Verse 26
durdyūtadevin gāndhāre nākṣān kṣipati gāṇḍivam jvalitān niśitāṃs tīkṣṇāñ śarān kṣipati gāṇḍivam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 29, Verse 33
yaudhiṣṭhirāṇy anīkāni pradahanti tatas tataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 30, Verse 2
ataḥ paraṃ raṇe sūta kim akurvanta māmakāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 31, Verse 2
ānantaryam abhiprepsuḥ ṣaḍviṃśatyā samārpayat punaś cāgnisamasparśair āśīviṣaviṣopamaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 31, Verse 12
kuñjarāṇāṃ ca saṃpāto babhūva kaṭukodayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 31, Verse 17
anīkānāṃ prabhagnānām avasthānam apaśyatām duṣkaraṃ pratisaṃdhānaṃ bhuvi cāsīt tadā nṛpa

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 31, Verse 25
cakreṇa cakram āsādya vīro vīrasya saṃyuge atīteṣupathe kāle jahāra gadayā śiraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 31, Verse 29
bhītaś cānya udakrośad anyo bhīta upādravat asaṃprāptasya taṃ deśam anyo jīvitam ādade

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 31, Verse 51
rāmaśiṣyo mahābāhur dhanvināṃ mānahā sadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 31, Verse 52
tathaivādhirathis tasya bāṇāñ jvalitatejasaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 31, Verse 67
pattyaśvarathamātaṅgās tvadīyāḥ śataśo 'pare karṇam evābhyadhāvanta trāsyamānāḥ prahāriṇaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 31, Verse 72
saṃrambheṇābhisaṃsṛjya nighnatām itaretaram kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca droṇārjunasamāgame

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 31, Verse 76
mahābale kṣubdhamahārṇavopame mahendrasadmātithitāṃ yiyāsavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 32, Verse 5
tato duryodhano rājā droṇaṃ dīno 'bhyabhāṣata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 32, Verse 19
saubhadraḥ pṛthivīpāla jahau prāṇān paraṃtapa mahārathaṃ śalyaputraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ ca tava priyam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 33, Verse 11
vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ abhimanyuṃ hataṃ śrutvā dhṛtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥ vistareṇa mahārāja paryapṛcchat sa saṃjayam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 33, Verse 12
kesarāṇi ca padmasya sukumārāṇi bhārata kumārā rājalokasya nikṣiptāḥ kesaropamāḥ karṇikāstho mahārāja tasya duryodhano 'bhavat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 33, Verse 14
candanāgurudigdhāṅgāḥ sragviṇaḥ sūkṣmavāsasaḥ sahitāḥ paryadhāvanta kārṣṇiṃ prati yuyutsavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 33, Verse 16
duryodhanas tu rājendra sainyamadhye vyavasthitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 33, Verse 20
tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ tumulaṃ lomaharṣaṇam tāvakānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 34, Verse 18
śṛṇu rājan mahābāho vacanaṃ mama suvrata purā garbhagate vāpi cakravyūhapraveśanam mukhāt kṛṣṇasya rājendra śrutam asmi mayā prabho tasmād vyūhaṃ praviśyāmi cakrākhyaṃ nṛpasattama

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 34, Verse 24
yāto 'ham arjunād rājan subhadrāyāṃ tathaiva ca mahadbalena saṃpūrṇaṃ paśyadhvaṃ pauruṣaṃ mama sarvān haniṣyāmi kurūn droṇamukhyān narādhipa yaiḥ kṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ karma pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām jyeṣṭhā mātā madīyā yat sabhāṃ nītā durāsadaiḥ duḥśāsanena ca tadā pāpena duṣṭakarmaṇā pāñcālāṃ prati rājendra yat kṛtaṃ duṣṭakāribhiḥ tat sarvaṃ cādya tadvyūhe darśayiṣyāmi lāghavāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 34, Verse 26
nāhaṃ pārthena jātaḥ syāṃ na ca jātaḥ subhadrayā yadi me saṃyuge kaś cij jīvito nādya mucyate yadi caikarathenāhaṃ samagraṃ kṣatramaṇḍalam na karomy aṣṭadhā yuddhe na bhavāmy arjunātmajaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 35, Verse 4
droṇo hi kṛtavān yatnaṃ śastrāstrakṛtaniśramaḥ tvaṃ tu bālaḥ sa balavān saṃgrāmāṇām akovidaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 35, Verse 5
vyavasāyo hi me yoddhuṃ raṇotsavasamudbhavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 35, Verse 6
yac caitat paśyase sūta sayodhāśvarathadvipam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 35, Verse 7
evam apy ucyamānaḥ sa sārathis taṃ punaḥ punaḥ vīra te tena mā yuddham iti saubhadram abravīt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 35, Verse 15
tad abhedyam anādhṛṣyaṃ droṇānīkaṃ sudurjayam bhittvārjunir asaṃbhrānto viveśācintyavikramaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 35, Verse 31
samāsthitān yodhavarair dāntāśvān sādhusārathīn vipatākādhvajacchattrān vitūṇīrāyudhān api visūtāśvarathābhīśūn viśamyāyoktradaṇḍakān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 35, Verse 40
yathāsurabalaṃ ghoraṃ tryambakenāmitaujasā kṛtvā karma raṇe 'sahyaṃ parair ārjunir āhave

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 36, Verse 3
abhimanyur asau vīro viṣṇutulyaparākramaḥ saubhadro ayam āyāto asmāñ jetuṃ mahābalaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 36, Verse 11
tato rathāḥ padātyoghāḥ kuñjarāḥ sādinaś ca ha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 36, Verse 21
abhyadravata taṃ kārṣṇim aśmakendraḥ kṛtatvaraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 36, Verse 35
saubhadraśaranirbhiṇṇāḥ samare 'maravikramāḥ evaṃ śalyo vimṛditas tava pautreṇa bhārata yudhyamāno mahābāhuḥ śakratulyaparākramaḥ jaghāna samare sarvān nānāśastraviśāradān itīva teṣāṃ samare mahātmā pratāpavān nītivatāṃ variṣṭhaḥ yuddhe ca tasmin sa mahābalo ripūṃś cakāra sarvān iṣubhiḥ pradagdhān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 37, Verse 22
tāṃs tathā dravato dṛṣṭvā saubhadraḥ prahasann iva

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 38, Verse 1
yat sainyaṃ mama putrasya mama pautraḥ prabādhate yathā caiva hi yat sainyaṃ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 38, Verse 16
abhimanyuṃ mahāsattvaṃ ślāghate vandino yathā tasmāt saṃpaśyatas tasya droṇācāryasya dhīmataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 38, Verse 21
duḥśāsanas tu saṃrabdhaṃ jñātvā bhrātaram agrajam tān nivartya rathodārān atha bhrātaram abravīt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 38, Verse 26
duḥśāsanas tathety ukto bhrātrā tava sutas tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 39, Verse 1
tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ tayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ tasmin kāle mahābāhuḥ saubhadraḥ paravīrahā saśaraṃ kārmukaṃ chittvā lāghavena nyapātayat duḥśāsanaṃ śarair ghoraiḥ saṃtatakṣa samantataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 39, Verse 3
akṣakūṭaṃ samāśritya saubalasyābhavad balam śṛṇu me vacanaṃ tāta pitṛvyo 'si mahāmate sauhṛdaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā sarvair eva durātmabhiḥ bhuktaṃ rājyam idaṃ mūḍhaiḥ sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtaiḥ suhṛdbhir bhujyate rājyaṃ suhṛdbhir bhujyate sukham vinā suhṛdbhir bhogāś ca aihikāmutrikaṃ ca yat mithyābhūtaṃ ca tat sarvaṃ suhṛdbhir varjitaṃ tadā dūrdyūtadevanā yūyaṃ pāpiṣṭhāḥ pāpavañcakāḥ teṣāṃ tvam agraṇīḥ pāpa yena sā drupadātmajā ānītā ca sabhāṃ sādhvī tasyedaṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam darśayiṣyāmi sarveṣāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca durātmanām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 39, Verse 10
śarair agnisamasparśair ākarṇasamacoditaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 39, Verse 19
tathā tu vartamāne vai saṃgrāme 'tibhayaṃkare

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 39, Verse 21
tataḥ karṇo yayau rājann abhimanyujighāṃsayā bālo 'yaṃ yudhyamāno 'yaṃ mayā yoddhum ihecchati enaṃ vadhiṣyāmi ripuṃ yathā vṛtraṃ śacīpatiḥ evam uktvā tu rādheyo rathārūḍho mahārathaḥ yayau yoddhuṃ mahāvīraḥ kurūṇāṃ tatra paśyatām pradhmāpya śaṅkhaṃ rādheyo mahāmeghaughanisvanam rathenābhyapatad vegād ādityasadṛśena vai dhanuṣā pūryamāṇena maurvīguṇavibhūṣiṇā śarair agniśikhākārair āśīviṣasamaprabhaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 39, Verse 29
tasmai cikṣepa niśitaṃ śaraṃ paramasaṃhitam sacchattradhvajayantāraṃ sāśvam āśu smayann iva karṇo 'pi cāsya cikṣepa bāṇān saṃnataparvaṇaḥ asaṃbhrāntaś ca tān sarvān agṛhṇāt phalgunātmajaḥ tato muhūrtāt karṇasya bāṇenaikena vīryavān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 40, Verse 5
karṇānujaṃ ca saṃprekṣya tāvakā vyathitābhavan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 40, Verse 8
tiṣṭha karṇa maheṣvāsa kṛpa duryodhaneti ca droṇasya krośato rājaṃs tad anīkam abhajyata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 40, Verse 24
yathā purā vahnisutaḥ surasainyeṣu vīryavān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 41, Verse 10
naivaṃ kṛtaṃ mahatkarma bhīṣmeṇājñāsiṣaṃ tathā sindhurāṭtanayas tv eko yathā pārthān avārayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 41, Verse 15
tasya cālpena kālena niyamena sutoṣitaḥ prīto maheśvaras tasmai varaṃ caivaṃ dadau tadā sa tu vavre varaṃ tatra pāṇḍaveyān ahaṃ raṇe vārayeyaṃ rathenaikaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 41, Verse 16
yam āhur ajitaṃ saṃkhye śaṅkhacakragadādharam viṣṇusahasramūrdhānaṃ sa kṛṣṇaḥ pāti phālgunam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 41, Verse 17
tenoktas tam ṛte pārthaṃ śarvas tasmai varaṃ dadau ekāham iti rājendra tatraivādarśanaṃ gataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 42, Verse 15
vivyadhuḥ śaravarṣeṇa samantān nṛpasattamāḥ saṃchādyamāno bahubhiḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathaiḥ na vivyathe mahārāja divyam astram upāśritaḥ chittvā ca tāñ śarān rājañ śaravarṣaiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ chādayām āsa tān sarvāṃs tad abhūd romaharṣaṇam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 44, Verse 8
saṃtrastā vāhinī tubhyaṃ naur ivāsīn mahārṇave

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 44, Verse 12
so 'bhimanyus tatas tasya chittvā praṇadato balī

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 44, Verse 24
bhinnānīkāś ca diṅmūḍhā bhūyaḥ saṃtrastacetasaḥ bhallair utkṛttaśirasaḥ paralokam athāviśan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 45, Verse 3
mūlaṃ hi sarvadharmāṇāṃ daivataṃ svargavāsinām sa kṛṣṇo daivataṃ yeṣāṃ kiṃ teṣāṃ duḥkhasaṃbhavaḥ karmaṇāṃ pratipanne 'rthe kālena pariṇāmite kā cintā mahatī bhūpa cintayā bādhyate jaḍaḥ kriyopakramitaḥ pūrvaṃ pariṇāmadṛśaḥ sukham tyāgaṃ vinā mahārāja samādhānaṃ na vidyate bhavāṃs tadrahito rājañ śṛṇuṣvācarite phalam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 45, Verse 4
gotranāmabhir anyonyaṃ krandanto jīvitaiṣiṇaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 45, Verse 6
tathā sarve samabhyetya saubhadraṃ drutam arpayan tathā vinihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā tava senām anāthavat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 45, Verse 7
saubhadreṇa mahārāja śakrapratimatejasā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 45, Verse 12
siṃhaśāvo vane yadvat puṇḍarīkaśiśuṃ yathā śṛṇu vākyaṃ mahābāho abhimanyo mahābala gaccha tvaṃ pāṇḍavāñ śīghraṃ mā yuddhaṃ kuru suvrata tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā abhimanyuḥ pratāpavān uvāca lakṣmaṇaṃ kruddhaḥ prahasann iva bhārata gamiṣyāmi ciraṃ bhrātaḥ sarvān etān nihatya vai pāṇḍavān prati cādyaiva iti satyaṃ vadāmi te

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 45, Verse 15
tasya cātikramaṃ dṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇo yuddhakovidaḥ yuddhaṃ cakre tadā tena śastrāstrair matimān nṛpa tayor yuddham atīvāsīd budhāṅgārakayor iva anyonyaṃ * jighāṃsator balavāsavayor iva śarajālair mahāghorair vivyadhus te parasparam lakṣmaṇo niśitair bāṇair daśabhiś ca stanāntare ājaghānārjuniṃ caiva tathā viddho 'bhimanyunā pañcabhiḥ pañcabhir bāṇair nijaghne rathavājinaḥ sārathim iṣuṇaikena dhvajaṃ caikeṣuṇāhanat tribhir bāṇair dhanuś chittvā ārjuniḥ sumahābalaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 47, Verse 3
saṃdhyānugataparyantaḥ śaradīva divākaraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 47, Verse 8
magadhādhipateś cāpi jayatsenasya vai śiraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 47, Verse 13
hṛdyasaṃbhrāntavad rājaṃs tad adbhutam ivābhavat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 47, Verse 20
vikarṣato dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ nāntaraṃ dṛśyate hi vai

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 47, Verse 25
hrīmattvāt kṣitipālānāṃ paśyatām adya ca dvija na me 'ṅga hīyate kiṃ cin na vai vāg eti māṃ tathā kumāravaravīrasya saṃtaptaparameṣubhiḥ bāṇair acchinnanirmuktaiḥ śalyair antargataṃ mama vicinvadbhir ivāsūn me śarīraṃ na vibhāvyate kaḥ kiṃ kiṃ sa dhanurvedo yenaikena vayaṃ jitāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 47, Verse 27
jyālakṣaṇaṃ mayā ceha nopadiṣṭaṃ tu phalgune

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 47, Verse 30
puraḥ sthitena kenāpi duḥśakyo jetum ārjuniḥ saṃdhānakṛtalakṣasya kiṃ cid vyākṣiptacetasaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 47, Verse 31
dṛṣṭvā saubhadram asyantam uccaiḥ śabdam akurvata naṣṭalakṣaḥ kumāro 'yaṃ hanyatāṃ hanyatām iti tasya cintayamānasya abhimanyor mahātmanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 47, Verse 34
maṇḍalāni suśikṣābhir gatapratyāgatāni ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 47, Verse 37
kṣurapreṇa mahātejās tvaramāṇaḥ sapatnajit

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 48, Verse 2
yadi pāṇitalād etac cakraṃ mucyeta phālguneḥ varadānān mātulasya viṣṇoś cakram ivāpatet

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 48, Verse 11
tato mahītalāt kārṣṇir viṣapīta iva skhalan samabhyadhāvad daṣṭauṣṭho dauḥśāsanim atha kṣitau so 'pi vegavatīṃ gṛhya gadām udyamya cārjunim kiṃcicchvāsas tu saubhadro dauḥśāsanim atāḍayat tāv ubhau bhrātarāv evaṃ gatau vaivasvatakṣayam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 48, Verse 12
devakalpo maheṣvāsaḥ kṣatraṃ dagdhvā mahāyaśāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 48, Verse 17
kākapakṣākliptakeśaṃ paugaṇḍam iti saṃjñitam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 48, Verse 26
niṣṭanadbhir atīvārtair udvamad rudhirasravaiḥ naraiḥ patadbhiḥ patitair avanis tv adhikaṃ babhau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 48, Verse 33
astaṃ gato 'yaṃ dyumaṇis tāpayitvā mahābalaḥ saubhadraḥ śatrudamanaḥ kiṃ jātaṃ na vidma vai evaṃ bruvāṇo nṛpatiḥ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ vyūhadvāraṃ samāsādya bāṣpapūryākulekṣaṇaḥ tac chrutvā ca hataṃ putraṃ kauravair jihmakāribhiḥ lokaiḥ saṃkathitaṃ sarvam abhimanyoḥ parākramam śrutvā ca tair hataṃ vīraṃ dhairyam ālambya satvaram paramaṃ sattvam ālambya pratyuvāca yudhāṃ varaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 48, Verse 38
akṣayāṃ gatim āsādya sa gataḥ śāśvatīḥ samāḥ aihikāmutriko dātā phalasyānyo na vidyate sa putro nihato me 'dya nāhaṃ jīvitum utsahe kiṃ mayā jīvitenārthaḥ saubhadreṇa vinā bhuvi

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 49, Verse 3
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ eṣa karṇaṃ kṛpaṃ śalyaṃ rājānaṃ ca suyodhanam droṇaṃ drauṇiṃ maheṣvāsaṃ tathaivānyān mahārathān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 49, Verse 4
cikrīḍitaṃ raṇe tena nighnatā vai parān varān kṛtāstrān yuddhakuśalān maheṣvāsān mahābalān kulaśīlaguṇair yuktāñ śūrān vikhyātapauruṣān droṇena vihitaṃ vyūham abhedyam amarair api adṛṣṭapūrvam asmābhiḥ padmaṃ cakrāyudhapriyaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 49, Verse 7
śūragrāhākulaṃ bhīmaṃ tīrtvā cainam abhītavat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 49, Verse 8
hatavatsāṃ yathā dhenuṃ taddarśanakṛtonmukhīm

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 50, Verse 0
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca atha saṃśaptakaiḥ sārdhaṃ yudhyamāne dhanaṃjaye abhimanyau hate cāpi bāle balavatāṃ vare maharṣisattame yāte vyāse sa tu yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kim athākārṣuḥ śokopahatacetasaḥ kathaṃ saṃśaptakebhyo vā nivṛtto vānaradhvajaḥ kena vā kathitas tasya praśāntaḥ sutapāvakaḥ etan me śaṃsa tattvena sarvam eveha saṃjaya śṛṇu rājan yathā tebhyo nivṛttaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ tataḥ sarvāṇi sainyāni dahan kṛṣṇagatir yathā saṃprayāte 'stam āditye saṃdhyākāla upasthite āyātasyātmaśibiraṃ nimittair aghaśaṃsibhiḥ yac cāsīn mānasaṃ tasya yac ca kṛṣṇena bhāṣitam yathā ca kathitas tasya nihataḥ sutapāvakaḥ vistareṇaiva me sarvaṃ bruvataḥ śṛṇu māriṣa

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 50, Verse 44
arjunaḥ kathaṃ tvayi ca bhīme ca dhṛṣṭadyumne ca jīvati sātyake śakravikrānte saubhadro nihataḥ paraiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 50, Verse 47
nānāliṅgaiḥ sudhautāgrair mama putro 'lpacetanaḥ iha me syād api trāṇaṃ piteti sa punaḥ punaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 50, Verse 52
subhadrāṃ nanu śocāmi yā putram apalāyinam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 50, Verse 53
śrutvā nipatitaṃ śūram anaghaṃ kṛtalāghavam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 50, Verse 60
saṃjaya uvāca putraśokārditaṃ pārthaṃ dhyāyantaṃ sāśrulocanam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 50, Verse 69
kālo grasati kaunteya viśvam etac carācaram nālaṃ buddhis tathāpy asya pumān vāpi virajyate utpattau ca vipattau ca karmaṇā galahastinā baddhaḥ śakuntavaj jīvo madhye svapnopamā gatiḥ na śocanti kṛtaprajñāḥ śvasatām upakalpanāt nūnaṃ jātena martavyaṃ kim u śocasi bālavat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 50, Verse 72
kṣipraṃ drakṣyanti me nūnaṃ mama putraṃ nihatya vai

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 50, Verse 74
sūnoḥ pāṇḍavapāñcālān agopsyaṃ taṃ mahāraṇe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 50, Verse 80
mahendram iva tiṣṭhantaṃ vajrodyatamahābhujam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 5
tatas tam apratiratham ahaṃ saubhadram abravam droṇānīkam idaṃ bhindhi dvāraṃ saṃjanayasva naḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 12
gadāhasto 'bhyayāt tūrṇaṃ jighāṃsur aparājitam gadinaṃ tv atha taṃ dṛṣṭvā vāsavasyātmajātmajaḥ sa jagrāha gadāṃ vīro gadāyuddhaviśāradaḥ gadāmaṇḍalamārgasthau sarvakṣatrasya paśyataḥ tau saṃprajahratur vīrāv anyonyasyāntaraiṣiṇau tāv anyonyaṃ gadāgrābhyāṃ tāḍitau yuddhadurmadau indradhvajāv ivotsṛṣṭau gatasattvau mahīṃ gatau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 13
aṣṭau rathasahasrāṇi nava dantiśatāni ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 14
tataḥ sma śokasaṃtaptā bhavatādya sameyuṣaḥ adīnas trāsayañ śatrūn nandayitvā ca bāndhavān asakṛn nāma viśrāvya pitṝṇāṃ mātulasya ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 16
vyathito nyapatad bhūmau duḥkhārtaḥ sa mumoha ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 19
triśikhāṃ bhrukuṭīṃ kṛtvā krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 22
mayi vismṛtasauhārdaṃ duryodhanahite ratam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 23
rājan droṇamukhāṃs tāṃs tān vārayiṣyāmy ahaṃ śaraiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 28
adattvā bhuñjatāṃ yā vai māṃsaṃ vā sā gatir mama

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 32
yaḥ pratyavasito vipro na saṃnyāsaṃ punaś caret prāyaścittena yasya syāc chuddhas tasya ca yā gatiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 33
tathā devalakāñ śrāddhe satataṃ paṅktidūṣakān ye bhojayanti saṃmūḍhās tāṃ gatiṃ samavāpnuyām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 34
matsyakacchapabhakṣāṇāṃ bhakṣyamastakaśāyinām saindhavānāṃ gatiṃ yāmi śvo na hanyāṃ jayadratham

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 37
anastamita āditye na ced dhanmi jayadratham

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 51, Verse 43
anṛtyad iva gāṇḍīvaṃ śarās tūṇīgatā mudā nirākrāmann iva tadā svayam eva mṛdhaiṣiṇaḥ bhīmasenas tu saṃhṛṣṭaḥ pratyabhāṣata bhārata dhanaṃjayam abhiprekṣya harṣagadgadayā girā pratijñodbhavaśabdena kṛṣṇaśaṅkhasvanena ca nihato dhārtarāṣṭro 'yaṃ sānubandhaḥ suyodhanaḥ atha mṛditatamāgryadāmamālyaṃ tava sutaśokamayaṃ ca roṣajātam vyapanudati mahāprabhāvam etan saṃjaya uvāca atha śaṅkhaiś ca bherībhiḥ paṇavaiḥ sainikās tathā sasūtamāgadhā jiṣṇuṃ stutibhiḥ samapūjayan tadā bhīmaṃ balaṃ sarvaṃ tena nādena mohitam tāvakaṃ tan mahārājaṃ viṣaṇṇaṃ samapadyata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 52, Verse 8
pratijñātaṃ na jānāmi sarvān vijñāpayāmi vaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 52, Verse 10
vaśam eṣyanti catvāras tam ṛte sarvapāṇḍavāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 52, Verse 12
vṛttam āsthāya tanyūjyaṃ (sic) sopanīto bhavāmy aham duḥśalā bhrātṛsauhārdān māṃ rakṣasyatha vā dhruvam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 52, Verse 14
eṣāṃ hi naradevānāṃ mattamātaṅgagāminām saṃghātam upayātānām api bibhyet puraṃdaraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 52, Verse 17
māyāvī balavāñ śūro rākṣasaś cāpy alambusaḥ ime ca tvābhigopsyanti sainyena mahatā vṛtāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 52, Verse 21
arjunasyātmanaś cārthe viśeṣaṃ paryapṛcchata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 52, Verse 33
tataḥ praharṣaḥ sainyānāṃ tavāpy āsīd viśāṃ pate vāditrāṇāṃ dhvaniś cograḥ siṃhanādaravaiḥ saha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 53, Verse 5
saṃśrute sindhurājasya vadhe gāṇḍīvadhanvanā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 53, Verse 11
bhṛśaṃ vimanaso bhūtvā śibirāṇi svakāni te

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 53, Verse 13
mama putra[tro] hato 'nena haniṣye 'haṃ jayadratham iti vāco bahuvidhā[ḥ] pārthena pratijñā kṛtā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 53, Verse 20
arjunasyāgrato yoddhuṃ bibhiyād api devarāṭ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 53, Verse 23

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 53, Verse 32
paśyatas te nihantāsmi yadi te vajradhāriṇaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 53, Verse 40

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 53, Verse 45

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 53, Verse 50
tava prasādād bhagavan kim ivāsti raṇe mama aviṣahyaṃ hṛṣīkeśa kiṃ jānan māṃ vigarhase

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 53, Verse 51
yathā rāmeṇa caikena sādhito daśakaṃdharaḥ vibhunā sādhayiṣyāmi tathā taṃ saindhavaṃ ripum

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 53, Verse 54
tvaṃ ca mādhava sarvaṃ tat tathā pratividhāsyasi yathā ripūṇāṃ miṣatāṃ pramathiṣyāmi saindhavam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 54, Verse 1
vāsudevārjunau vīrau na svapnam upalebhatuḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 54, Verse 7

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 54, Verse 17
svādhyāyayuktaṃ brāhmaṇī yācitāraṃ gaurvoḍhāraṃ tv āśugantāram aśvā dāsaṃ śūdrā karmakaraṃ tu vaiśyā śūraṃ sūte tvadvidhā rājaputrī

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 55, Verse 9
yatra tvaṃ keśave nāthe satyanātho yathā hataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 55, Verse 11
ehy ehi tṛṣito vatsa stanau pūrṇau pibāśu me aṅkam āruhya mandāyā hy atṛptāyāś ca darśane

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 55, Verse 14
sākṣān maghavataḥ pautraṃ putraṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ svasrīyaṃ vāsudevasya taṃ gṛdhrāḥ paryupāsate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 55, Verse 17
uttarām uttarāṃ jātyā suśīlāṃ priyabhāṣiṇīm śanakaiḥ parirabhyaināṃ snuṣāṃ mama yaśasvinīm sukumārīṃ viśālākṣīṃ pūrṇacandranibhānanām bālapallavatanvaṅgīṃ mattamātaṅgagāminīm bimbādharoṣṭhīm abalām abhimanyo praharṣaya tvayā vinā kathaṃ putra jīrṇāṃ patitamānasām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 55, Verse 23
brāhmaṇebhyaḥ śaraṇyebhyo nidhiṃ nidadhatāṃ ca yā yā cāpi nyastadaṇḍānāṃ tāṃ gatiṃ vraja putraka

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 55, Verse 27
kṛcchreṣu yā dhārayatām ātmānaṃ vyasaneṣu ca gatiḥ śokāgnidagdhānāṃ tāṃ gatiṃ vraja putraka pitur mātuś ca śuśrūṣāṃ kalpayantīha ye sadā svadāraniratānāṃ ca yā gatis tām avāpnuhi

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 55, Verse 33
draupadī śokasaṃtaptā ruditvā ca vilapya ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 56, Verse 10
sa ca rājā mahāvīryaḥ pārayatv arjunaḥ satām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 56, Verse 12
yady asti sukṛtaṃ kiṃ cid asmākaṃ hantu saindhavam jitvā sarvān ripūn pārthas trātuṃ no 'smān mahābhayāt evam āśaṃsamānās te ke cit tasthur upaśrutim śrutvā ceṣṭaṃ sumanaso vyaktam āśaṃsire jayam bhavitā nu kathaṃ kṛtyam idam ity apare 'bruvan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 56, Verse 13
mahad dhi sāhasaṃ pārthaḥ kṛtavāñ śokamohitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 56, Verse 14
arjune hi jayas teṣām āyatto jīvitāni ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 56, Verse 28
adya jñāsyanti tridaśāḥ sāsurāḥ sacarācarāḥ vāsudevasya tāṃ prītiṃ pāṇḍaveṣv anapāyinīm

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 2
niśvasantaṃ mahātmānaṃ saphenam iva pannagam visaṃjñamanasaṃ jñātvā arjunaṃ śokavihvalam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 7
yat tu kāryaṃ bhavet kāryaṃ karmaṇā tat samācara hīnaceṣṭasya yaḥ śokaḥ sa hi śatrur dhanaṃjaya

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 12
hatāvaśeṣās tatremā daśa mādhava saṃkhyayā tābhiḥ parivṛtaḥ saṃkhye sarvaiś caiva mahārathaiḥ kathaṃ śakyeta sa draṣṭuṃ durātmā kṛṣṇa saindhavaḥ pratijñāpāraṇaṃ caiva na bhaviṣyati keśava

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 44
tam evāgniṃ tam ādityaṃ bhūyo bhūyas tatheśvaram yajurvedavidaś caivādityavarṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastāt gāyanti yaṃ sāmavida ihaiva iti nihnutam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 45
śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ devam īśānaṃ parameśvaram jagāma jagatāṃ nātham arjunaḥ sajanārdanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 46
**** **** naranārāyaṇāv ubhau suprasannamanāḥ śarvaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 48

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 51
pinākine haviṣyāya satyāya vibhave sadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 55
abhigamyāya kāmyāya stutyāyāryāya sarvadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 58
namo 'stu devadevāya mahābhūtadharāya ca mīḍhuṣṭamāya havyāya śraviṣṭāya śrutāya ca śipiviṣṭāya giraye namo budhyāya vilmine namaḥ parṇāya gehyāya druhyāya prabhṛśāya ca namaḥ parṇāya śuṣkāya rajasyāya pulastyaye duṃdubhyāya hananyāya svāyudhāya sudhanvane namaḥ stutyāya pathyāya kāvyāyāśurathāya ca namaḥ somyāya vātyāya urvayāya niṣaṅgiṇe vaiśantāya ca kūpyāya nīpāya ca varūthine namaḥ somāya rudrāya tāmrāya śivamūrtaye

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 59
arjunāya dadau buddhiṃ tasminn astre yad īpsitam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 63
svāgataṃ vāṃ naraśreṣṭha vijñātaṃ manasepsitam yena kāmena saṃprāptau bhavadbhyāṃ taṃ dadāmy aham

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 79
tataḥ pāśupataṃ divyam avāpya punar īśvarāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 80
tato 'rjunahṛṣīkeśau punaḥ punar ariṃdamau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 57, Verse 81
tathā bhavenānumatau mahāsuranighātinau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 58, Verse 10
rājahaṃsanibhaṃ prāpya uṣṇīṣaṃ śithilārpitam jalakṣayanimittaṃ vai veṣṭayām āsa mūrdhani

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 58, Verse 11
kṛtvendriyāṇām aikāgryaṃ manasaś ca mahāmanāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 58, Verse 24

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 58, Verse 32
praveśyatāṃ samīpaṃ me kimarthaṃ pravilambase

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 59, Verse 0
saṃjaya uvāca tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā pratinandya janārdanam uvāca paramaprītaḥ kaunteyo devakīsutam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 59, Verse 2
darśanād eva te saumya na kiṃ cid aśubhaṃ mama

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 59, Verse 3

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 59, Verse 4
yudhāmanyuṃ subāhuṃ ca draupadeyāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 59, Verse 5
sthiteṣv adhiparārdhyeṣu yathārhaṃ vaṃdya pārthivam anujñātāś ca pārthena āsīnā āsaneṣu te

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 59, Verse 13
yathaiva sarvāsv āpatsu pāsi vṛṣṇīñ janārdana tathaivāsmān mahābāho vṛjināt trātum arhasi tvam agādhe 'plave magnān pāṇḍavān kurusāgare samuddhara plavo bhūtvā śaṅkhacakragadādhara namaste devadeveśa sanātana viśātana viṣṇo jiṣṇo hare kṛṣṇa vaikuṇṭhapuruṣottama nāradas tvāṃ samācakhyau purāṇam ṛṣisattamam varadaṃ śārṅgiṇaṃ devaṃ tat satyaṃ kuru mādhava ity uktaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣo dharmarājena saṃsadi toyameghasvano vāgmī pratyuvāca yudhiṣṭhiram

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 60, Verse 13
rathaṃ puruṣasiṃhasya sadhvajaṃ sapatākinam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 60, Verse 21
dhanur jaitraṃ tathā bāṇān dadhāno nirgato 'rjunaḥ hantuṃ laṃkāpatiṃ devo bhagavān iva rāghavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 60, Verse 24
tatas tasmin kṣaṇe rājan vividhāni śubhāni ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 60, Verse 28
gaccha tvaṃ rakṣa rājānaṃ tvaṃ hi tulyo mayā raṇe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 60, Verse 30
na hi paśyāmi taṃ loke yas tvāṃ yuddhe parājayet vāsudevasamaṃ yuddhe svayam apy amareśvaraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 61, Verse 6
bhūyāñ śabdān atīvānyāñ śabdaḥ saindhavaveśmani paurāṇikānāṃ tūryāṇāṃ śaṅkhadundubhighoṣavān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 61, Verse 23
saṃśāmya bhrātṛbhis tais tu kṣatriyān abhipālaya

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 61, Verse 24
karṇaduḥśāsanamate saubalasya ca durmateḥ pratyākhyāto mahābāhuḥ kulāntakaraṇena me

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 61, Verse 26
**** **** viduro droṇa eva vā bāhlikaḥ somadatto vā bhīṣmo droṇāyanis tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 61, Verse 27

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 61, Verse 28

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 61, Verse 31

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 61, Verse 45
senāṃ dṛṣṭvābhibhūtāṃ me śaineyenārjunena ca śūnyān dṛṣṭvā rathopasthān manye śocanti putrakāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 62, Verse 2
prathamaṃ śiro muṇḍayitvā paścān nakṣatrapṛcchanam kiṃ karoṣi ca tvaṃ rājan kālo hi duratikramaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 62, Verse 8
aprāptaḥ sa mahad dharmaṃ kāmam arthaṃ yaśas tathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 62, Verse 17

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 63, Verse 5
dṛśyante kuñjaraiś cānyair vājibhiś ca yuyutsavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 63, Verse 29
tasya sarvasya sainyasya netā goptā ca vīryavān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 64, Verse 4
piśitāsṛgbhujāṃ saṃghāḥ pralīyante sahasraśaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 64, Verse 5

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 64, Verse 12
tiṣṭhadhvaṃ rathino yūyaṃ saṃgrāmam abhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ yudhyāmi saṃhatān etān yaśo mānaṃ ca vardhayan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 64, Verse 13
tato 'rjuno mahārāja pratyadṛśyata bhārata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 64, Verse 27
durmarṣaṇabalaṃ pūrvam atha duḥśāsanānugam tataḥ śakaṭasaṃsthaṃ ca ghoranādasamākulam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 64, Verse 35
**** **** amarṣād bhrukuṭīkṛtaiḥ tathaiva krodhadaṣṭoṣṭhair avākīryata medinī

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 64, Verse 39
gṛhītvānyasya keśeṣu śiro nṛtyati cāparaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 64, Verse 42
tiṣṭha pārthair hi māṃ pārtha kva yāsīti ca jalpatām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 65, Verse 7
yuvarājo balaślāghī piṅgalaḥ priyadarśanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 65, Verse 11
tadācalaghanaprakhyaṃ patākāśatasaṃkulam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 65, Verse 12
dhanaṃjayaśarodvignāḥ palāyanto babhur gajāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 65, Verse 14

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 65, Verse 16
puṅkhāvaśiṣṭair bahubhiḥ śoṇitotpīḍavāhinaḥ yugapac ca samāviṣṭair

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 65, Verse 22
tato 'rjuno bhṛśaṃ kruddhaḥ pradahann iva tejasā vavarṣa śaravarṣāṇi yodhānām anivartinām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 65, Verse 31
evaṃ bale drute yāte rājaputraṃ mahāratham vivyādha daśabhir bāṇais tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt jīvitena kathaṃ gantā duruktaṃ yāvad adya te tad vākyasadṛśaṃ karma kuru tvaṃ yadi manyase evam uktvā tato rājan pārthaḥ pārthivamardanaḥ bhṛśaṃ kruddho mahārāja avidhyat tanayaṃ tava

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 66, Verse 7
yathā tvaṃ bhāṣase pārtha mamāpy evaṃ mataṃ vibho kiṃ tu svāmyarthayuktais tu kāryaṃ yuddhaṃ manīṣibhiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 66, Verse 27
tatrādbhutam apaśyāma śilānām iva sarpaṇam yad droṇaṃ tarasā pārtho vṛddhaṃ bālo 'pi nātarat cintayām āsa vārṣṇeyo dṛṣṭvā droṇasya vikramam nātivartiṣyate hy enaṃ velām iva mahārṇavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 66, Verse 28
tataḥ pārthaṃ samudvignaṃ lakṣya cintayate 'cyutaḥ droṇasya cāpi vikrāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā madhunighātanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 67, Verse 12
**** **** śaravarṣeṇa vīryavān avārayad asaṃbhrānto na tv ācāryam apīḍayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 67, Verse 35
dra[drā]vyamāṇeṣu sainyeṣu pāṇḍavena tatas tataḥ śrutāyudho mahātejāḥ kiran bāṇān samabhyayāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 67, Verse 50
hanyād eṣā pratīpaṃ hi prayoktāram iti prabho na cākarot sa tadvākyaṃ prāpte kāle śrutāyudhaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 67, Verse 52
tato 'rjunaḥ kṣuraprābhyāṃ bhujau parighasaṃnibhau vivyādha pāṇḍavaḥ śīghraṃ jaleśvarasutasya vai sā jvalantī maholkeva samāsādya janārdanam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 67, Verse 53
gadāṃ nivartitāṃ dṛṣṭvā nihataṃ ca śrutāyudham sa bhagna iva vātena bahuśākho vanaspatiḥ sā visphurantī jvalitā vajravegasamā gadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 67, Verse 65
śaktyā cābhihato gāḍhaṃ mūrchayābhipariplutaḥ samāśvāsya mahātejāḥ sṛkkiṇī parilelihan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 67, Verse 69
dhārayann agnisaṃkāśāṃ śirasā kāñcanīṃ srajam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 67, Verse 70
mahārhābharaṇopetaḥ sānumān iva parvataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 68, Verse 5
uccakarta śirāṃsy ugro nāḷebhya iva paṅkajān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 68, Verse 41
kākavarṇā durācārāḥ strīlolāḥ kalahapriyāḥ drāviḍās tatra yudhyante mattavāraṇavāraṇāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 68, Verse 43
abhyavarṣanta te sarve pāṇḍavaṃ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ avākiraṃś ca te mlecchā nānāyuddhaviśāradāḥ teṣām api sasarjāśu śaravṛṣṭiṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 68, Verse 49
tathāsīd āplutā dhātrī rudhireṇa viśāṃ pate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 68, Verse 56
tataḥ prāvartata nadī śoṇitasya taraṅgiṇī narāśvadvipakāyebhyaḥ parvatebhya ivāpagā asthiśarkarasaṃbādhā dhvajavṛkṣā rathahradā saṃchinnaśīrṣapāṣāṇā hastihastamahāgrahā māṃsamajjāsthipaṅkāḍhyā hatāśvamakarākulā yodhagomāyusaṃkīrṇā kabandhaśatasaṃkulā uṣṇīṣaphenasaṃchannā śaraghorajhaṣākulā rudrasyākrīḍasadṛśīṃ bhūmiṃ kurvan vibhīṣaṇām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 68, Verse 58
gadāpāṇir drutaṃ yātvā pragṛhya mahatīṃ gadām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 68, Verse 65
ambaṣṭhe tu tadā bhagne tava sainyam abhajyata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 68, Verse 66
ādadānaṃ śaraiḥ prāṇān gajāśvarathasādinām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 69, Verse 14
**** **** vacasā lalitaṃ sadā hṛdayena bhṛśaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 69, Verse 40
sa saṃyukto mahābāhur ācāryeṇa mahātmanā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 69, Verse 46
yena devāḥ sakṛdbhagnāḥ saṃgrāme tārakāmaye dhṛtāḥ sa cāhataḥ śūro hy avadhyo devatāgaṇaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 69, Verse 47
diśaś ca vidiśaś caiva svasti tubhyaṃ prakurvatām prajānāṃ patayaś caiva siddhā lokahite ratāḥ svasti kurvantu te nityaṃ mantreṇānena saṃstutāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 69, Verse 50
vihvalā hṛtavīryāś ca sahendrā vibudhā drutāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 69, Verse 64
sa tena varmaṇā gupto vṛtraṃ devaripuṃ tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 69, Verse 65
jaghāna samare 'bhītaḥ śakro devāgraṇīs tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 69, Verse 68
**** **** tasya karma babandha ca uvāca cainam ācāryas tava putram idaṃ vacaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 69, Verse 69
brahmaṇaś ca svasūktena badhnāmi kavacaṃ tava

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 69, Verse 72
prasthitaḥ sahasā rājan yatra yāto dhanaṃjayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 69, Verse 74
**** **** nānājanapadāyutaḥ tava putraḥ prayātas tu

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 70, Verse 4
rājan na tādṛśaṃ yuddhaṃ dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ na ca śrutam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 70, Verse 31
hanyamānaṃ tu tat sainyaṃ bhāradvājena sarvataḥ śarair agniśikhākārair dahyate bharatarṣabha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 70, Verse 47
evaṃ dvaṃdvaśatāny āsaṃs tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 71, Verse 9
āvantyau bhrātarau śūrau dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayudhyatām sālvako bilvakaś cobhau yathā viṣṇuṃ kṛte yuge

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 71, Verse 10
na sma vijñāyate rājan nāpy anyo bubudhe kriyām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 72, Verse 9
tāvakāḥ samare yodhāḥ pāṇḍaveyāś ca vikṣatāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 72, Verse 30
dhṛṣṭadyumnāya cikṣepa śacīpatir ivāśanim

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 73, Verse 10
evam uktas tataḥ sūtaḥ satyakasyāvahad ratham

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 73, Verse 11
tatas tau droṇaśaineyau yuyudhāte paraṃtapau śarair anekasāhasrais tāḍayantau parasparam iṣujālāvṛtaṃ vyoma cakratuḥ puruṣarṣabhau pūrayām āsatur vīrāv ubhau daśa diśaḥ śaraiḥ meghāv ivātapāpāye dhārābhir itaretaram na sma sūryas tadā bhāti na vavau ca samīraṇaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 73, Verse 12
andhakārīkṛte loke droṇaśaineyayoḥ śaraiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 73, Verse 19
nikṛntatoḥ śarais tīkṣṇair droṇasatyakayos tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 73, Verse 23
sarvataḥ parivāryobhau pratatākṣabhivīkṣire

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 73, Verse 30
gandharvā dānavā yakṣā rākṣasāpsarasaḥ khagāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 73, Verse 35
evam ekaśataṃ chinnaṃ dhanuṣāṃ dṛḍhadhanvinā na cāntaraṃ tayor dṛṣṭaṃ saṃdhāne chedane 'pi ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 73, Verse 39
siddhacāraṇasaṃghāś ca sādhu sādhv iti cukruśuḥ tuṣṭuvur lāghavāt tasya devāḥ sāgnipurogamāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 73, Verse 44
ity āsīt tumulaḥ śabdo durdharṣasya rathaṃ prati

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 73, Verse 53
tenāntareṇa pārthas tu raṇe jitvā mahārathān atikrāntas tadā yuddhaṃ kṛtvā paryavatasthivān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 74, Verse 1
vartamāne tathā yuddhe droṇasya saha pāṇḍubhiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 74, Verse 16
śrameṇa mahatā yuktās te hayā vātaraṃhasaḥ mandavegagatā rājan saṃvṛttās tatra saṃyuge

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 74, Verse 23
tau tu śastrabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃtoṣya bhārata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 74, Verse 25
nihato rudhirāktāṅgaḥ kampayann iva medinīm

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 74, Verse 46
tataḥ pārthas tv ajetavyo mahābāhubalāśrayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 74, Verse 53
dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca arjune dharaṇīṃ prāpte hayahaste ca keśave etad antaram āsādya kathaṃ pārtho na nirjitaḥ sadyaḥ pārthiva pārthena niruddhāḥ sarvapārthivāḥ rathasthā dharaṇīsthena vākyam acchāndasaṃ yathā bhūmistho 'pi rathasthāṃs tān pārthaḥ sarvadhanurdharān eko nivārayām āsa lobhaḥ sarvaguṇān iva

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 74, Verse 56
evaṃ pārthas tataś cakre vājināṃ ca saraḥ śubham savistīrṇaṃ prasannāmbhaḥ praphullavarapaṅkajam kūrmamatsyagaṇākīrṇam agādham ṛṣisevitam bhagavan nāradamuner darśanārthaṃ kṛtaṃ kṣaṇāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 75, Verse 11
saṃjayaḥ tatrādbhutataraṃ manye tat sainyaṃ tāvakaṃ prabho dadhāraikau raṇe pārtho velodvṛttam ivārṇavam pārthasya śarasaṃchanne sainye mahati bhārata ākāśam iva saṃprāpya vicerus tatra pakṣiṇaḥ na cainaṃ yudhi tiṣṭhantaṃ tava sainyeṣu māriṣa abhyadravata saṃkruddhaḥ pumān kaś cit tu tāvakaḥ sarve vimanaso bhūtvā tava yaudhā viśāṃ pate saṃprekṣya tatra govindaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 75, Verse 13
upāvṛtyotthitān aśvān pāṇibhyāṃ puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ saṃmārjayad raṇe rājan paśyatāṃ sarvayodhinām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 75, Verse 17
yojayitvā hayāṃs tatra vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā raṇe cacāra govindas tṛṇīkṛtya mahārathān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 75, Verse 19
tatsenāḥ sarvato hṛṣṭā lomaharṣaṇam adbhutam tvaradhvam iti cākrandan naitad astīti cābruvan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 75, Verse 21
yathā devāsure yuddhe tṛṇīkṛtya sadānavān indrāviṣṇū purā rājañ jambhasya vadhakāṅkṣiṇau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 75, Verse 31
preṣamāṇo jayatu hi yiyāsūn api raṃhasā amoghāḥ śatruhantāro vimalāḥ krośapātinaḥ manojavās te 'pi raṇe vājino javasaṃpadā kṛṣṇapratodatunnānāṃ rathavṛndānuśālinām viśeṣitāḥ prayogāc ca sarvaśatrunibarhaṇāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 76, Verse 28
mahāśailoccayāṃ ghorāṃ laṅghayitvā mahānadīm nistīrṇāv adhvagau yadvat tadvat tau tāritau raṇe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 77, Verse 21
apy ahaṃ tāni duḥkhāni pūrvavṛttāni mādhava duryodhanaṃ raṇe hatvā pratimokṣye kathaṃ cana

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 78, Verse 5
vaiphalyaṃ cāgatān bāṇāñ chinnān parapuraṃjayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 78, Verse 19

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 78, Verse 21

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 78, Verse 29
prayatnakārī kaunteyo nakhamāṃsāntareṣubhiḥ sa vedanābhir āvignaḥ palāyanaparāyaṇaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 78, Verse 37
tenācyutoṣṭhayugapūritamārutena śaṅkhāntarodaravivṛddhaviniḥsṛtena nādena sāsuraviyat suralokapālam udvignam īśvarajagat sphuṭatīva sarvam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 80, Verse 4
anekavarṇā vividhā dhvajāḥ paramaśobhinaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 81, Verse 20

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 82, Verse 12

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 82, Verse 18

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 82, Verse 37

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 83, Verse 27
jaghāna pāṇḍuputrasya sainikān raṇamūrdhani śaktayaḥ kaṇapāḥ prāsāḥ śūlapaṭṭiśatomarāḥ śataghnyaḥ parighāś caiva bhiṇḍipālāḥ paraśvadhāḥ śilāḥ khaḍgā guḍāś caiva ṛṣṭir vajrāṇi caiva ha sā rākṣasavisṛṣṭā tu śastravṛṣṭiḥ sudāruṇā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 83, Verse 29
sa hatvā rathabhūyiṣṭhāṃ nadīṃ prāvartayat tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 83, Verse 30

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 83, Verse 32

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 84, Verse 3

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 84, Verse 15
tasya nādena mahatā kampiteyaṃ vasuṃdharā saparvatavanā rājan sapādapajalāśayā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 84, Verse 21
rathād ratham abhidrutya kruddho haiḍimba ākṣipat udbabarha rathāc cāpi pannagaṃ garuḍo yathā samīkṣya tadavasthaṃ taṃ vadhāyāsya mano dadhe vegaṃ cakre mahāntaṃ ca rākṣasendrarathaṃ prati

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 84, Verse 24
pāṇḍavānāṃ tataḥ senā taṃ dṛṣṭvā vinipātitam nanāda sumahānādaṃ harṣavegasamāplutā tatas tu nipapātāśu gatāsur bhuvi rākṣasaḥ śikharaṃ parvatasyeva vajravegena pātitam patatā tena mahatā rathināṃ dantināṃ daśa tava sainye mahārāja nihatāḥ subṛhattayā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 84, Verse 29
tato ghaṭotkaco hatvā tad rakṣo vṛtrasaṃnibham punaḥ svaratham āsthāya vijigīṣur nanāda ca nanāda cātīva hi pāṇḍavātmajo raṇājire hṛṣṭamanā ghaṭotkacaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 84, Verse 30
tato 'bhigamya rājānaṃ dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram svakarmāvedayan mūrdhnā sāñjalir nipapāta ha mūrdhny upāghrāya taṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ pariṣvajya ca pāṇḍavaḥ prīto 'smīty abravīd rājan harṣād utphullalocanaḥ ghaṭotkacena niṣpiṣṭe mṛte sālakaṭaṅkaṭe babhūvur muditāḥ sarve hate tasmin niśācare

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 85, Verse 15
droṇaṃ vāraya sukṣipraṃ satyakaṃ mā vadhīd dvijaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 85, Verse 29
pāñcāleṣv atha śūreṣu kekayeṣu ca mānavāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 85, Verse 38

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 85, Verse 49

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 85, Verse 89

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 85, Verse 92
sadevāsuragandharvān sakiṃnaramahoragān yodhayet sa jagat sarvaṃ vijayeta ripūn bahūn iti bruvanti lokeṣu janās tava guṇās tathā samāgameṣu jalpanti pṛthag eva ca sarvadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 86, Verse 12
sa evaṃ vai vinikṣipto nikṣepaḥ savyasācinā bhāradvājabhayaṃ te 'dya manyate vai dhanaṃjayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 86, Verse 15
sa tvam adya raṇe yatto rakṣa mādhava pāṇḍavam rakṣaṇe dharmarājasya dhruvo hi vijayo mama

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 86, Verse 36

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 86, Verse 37

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 86, Verse 42

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 86, Verse 49

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 87, Verse 3
yathedānīm iti dhyātvā dharmarājam athābravīt śokagadgadayā vācā śokopahatacetanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 87, Verse 35
āsthitā dasyubhis tīkṣṇaiḥ śūrair uttamapārvataiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 87, Verse 39

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 87, Verse 51
triyojanagatasyāhaṃ padavīṃ savyasācinaḥ yāsyāmi rathināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ pravaraṃ ca dhanuṣmatām sūryodayagatasyāhaṃ pāṇḍavasya gatiṃ caran apareṇa gate sūrye gamiṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 87, Verse 64
āśiṣo vipulāḥ śrutvā dharmarājamukhodgatāḥ harṣeṇa mahatā yuktas tv āruroha rathottamam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 87, Verse 65
yathā śakrarathaṃ rājann ūhus te harayaḥ purā tathaiva bhīmaseno 'pi dharmarājena pūjitaḥ prāyāt sātyakinā sārdham abhivādya yudhiṣṭhiram tau dṛṣṭvā pravivikṣantau tava senām ariṃdamau saṃyattās tāvakāḥ sarve tasthur droṇapurogamāḥ saṃnaddham anugacchantaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmaṃ sa sātyakiḥ abhinandyābravīd vīras tadā harṣakaraṃ vacaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 87, Verse 72
apramādaś ca te kāryo droṇaṃ prati mahāratham

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 2
prayāte mādhave rājann idaṃ vacanam abravīt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 4
senāpativacaḥ śrutvā pāṇḍaveyāḥ samantataḥ abhyudyayur mahārāja tava sainyaṃ samantataḥ jahi prahara gṛhṇīhi vidhya vidrāva cādrava

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 5
bāṇaśabdaravān kṛtvā vimiśrāñ śaṅkhanisvanaiḥ yuyudhānarathaṃ dṛṣṭvā tāvakā abhidudruvuḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 7
athānyān api rājendra nānājanapadeśvarān śarair analasaṃkāśair ninye vīrān yamakṣayam śatam ekena vivyādha śatenaikaṃ ca patriṇām dvipārohān dvipāṃś caiva hayārohān hayāṃs tathā rathinaḥ sāśvasūtāṃś ca jaghāneśaḥ paśūn iva taṃ tathādbhutakarmāṇaṃ śarasaṃpātavarṣiṇam na ke canābhyadhāvan vai sātyakiṃ tava sainikāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 8
tam ekaṃ bahudhā paśyan mohitās tasya tejasā saṃgrāmakovidaṃ vīraṃ vicarantam abhītavat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 24
droṇas tu paramakruddhaḥ sātyakiṃ paravīrahā avākirac chitair bāṇair vāsudevaparākramam taṃ tathā śarajālena pracchādya mahatā punaḥ droṇaḥ prahasya śaineyam idaṃ vacanam abravīt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 27
ācāryānugato mārgaḥ śiṣyair anvāsyate sadā tasmād evaṃ vrajāmy āśu yathā me sa gurur gataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 30
abhedyam aribhir vīraiḥ sumahadbhir mahad balam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 32
deśasākalyam āsādya dṛśyate sumahad balam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 35
tataḥ śakyo mahāvyūho bhettuṃ sma sahasā raṇe taṃ deśaṃ tvaritā yāmo mṛdanto yudhi śātravān tatraite saṃprahṛṣṭatvān nāsmān prati yuyutsavaḥ ayudhyamāno bahubhir ekaṃ prāpya sudurbalam balaṃ pramathya gacchāmi miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvinām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 36
yatraite paramakruddhā dākṣiṇātyā mahārathāḥ etān vijitya saṃgrāme tato yāmo dhanaṃjayam yuyudhānavacaḥ śrutvā yuyudhānasya sārathiḥ yathoktam agamad rājan varjayan droṇam āhave

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 37
sa ca sainyaṃ mahad bhittvā dākṣiṇātyabalaṃ ca tat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 38
satyako hi tataḥ sainyaṃ drāvayan sa samantataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 39
vidrute tu bale tasmin bhagne bhārata bhārate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 48
te śarāḥ sātvatenāstāḥ kṛtavarmāṇam āhave chādayāṃ cakrire vṛkṣaṃ śalabhā iva ghoṣiṇaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 88, Verse 59
hārdikyaṃ samare yattā na śekuḥ prativīkṣitum

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 89, Verse 6
carmanistriṃśayuddhe ca niyuddhe ca viśāradam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 89, Verse 11
prabhinnakaraṭaiś caiva dviradair āvṛtaṃ mahat yad ahanyata me sainyaṃ kim anyad bhāgadheyataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 89, Verse 35
mahānāgān vidravato dṛṣṭvārjunaśarāhatān patitān patataś cānyān manye śocanti putrakāḥ hayaughān nihatān dṛṣṭvā drāvyamāṇāṃs tatas tataḥ raṇe sātvatapārthābhyāṃ manye śocanti putrakāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 90, Verse 1
purā yad ucyase prājñaiḥ suhṛdbhir vidurādibhiḥ māhārṣīḥ pāṇḍavān rājann iti tan na tvayā śrutam suhṛdāṃ hitakāmānāṃ vākyaṃ yo na śṛṇoti ha sa mahad vyasanaṃ prāpya śocate vai yathā bhavān yācito 'si purā rājan dāśārheṇa śamaṃ prati na ca taṃ labdhavān kāmaṃ tvattaḥ kṛṣṇo mahāyaśāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 90, Verse 2
tava jihmam abhiprāyaṃ viditvā pāṇḍavān prati

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 90, Verse 4

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 90, Verse 8

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 90, Verse 30
**** **** nistriṃśaṃ ca mahāprabham kṛtavarmāṇam uddiśya preṣayat tam asiṃ drutam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 90, Verse 34
