// Parva 7, Adhyaya 90, Verse 50
lajjayāvanatā bhūtvā na kiṃ cit pravadanti te

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 91, Verse 3
uvāca sārathiṃ tatra krodhāmarṣasamanvitaḥ hārdikyābhimukhaṃ sūta kuru me ratham uttamam kurute kadanaṃ paśya pāṇḍusainye hy amarṣitaḥ enaṃ jitvā punaḥ sūta yāsyāmi vijayaṃ prati evam ukte tu vacane sūtas tasya mahāmate nimeṣāntaramātreṇa kṛtavarmāṇam abhyayāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 91, Verse 8
palāyanakṛtotsāhā bhramantī tatra tatra ha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 91, Verse 17
mārutasya gatau tulyāś candrakundanibhāḥ śubhāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 91, Verse 23
kṣaranto 'sṛk tathā mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca pradudruvuḥ babhramuś caskhaluś cānye petur mamlus tathāpare evaṃ tat kuñjarānīkaṃ yuyudhānena pātitam śarair agnyarkasaṃkāśaiḥ pradudrāva samantataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 91, Verse 25
raktacandanadigdhāṅgaḥ sāṅgadaḥ sahakuṇḍalaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 91, Verse 29
saṃprāpayad raṇe rājan nāgarājaṃ mahābalam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 91, Verse 30
avidhyan niśitair bāṇaiḥ satyakaḥ prahasann iva

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 91, Verse 41
bhrājati sma tataḥ khaḍgaḥ saṃprāptaḥ pṛthivītalam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 91, Verse 42
jalasaṃdham abhiprekṣya utsmayitvā ca mādhavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 91, Verse 47
kabandhaṃ dviradaṃ caiva śaravarṣair avākirat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 91, Verse 52
jalasaṃdhaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā putras te kurupuṃgavaḥ sahodarais tu saṃyuktaḥ sātyakiṃ samupādravat tataḥ samabhavad yuddhaṃ kurūṇāṃ satyakasya ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 92, Verse 1
sātvatasya raṇe karma yoddhuṃ dṛṣṭvā mahārathāḥ amṛṣyamāṇāḥ saṃyattāḥ śaineyaṃ samupādravan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 92, Verse 6
sātyakiḥ puṇḍarīkākṣo hy astreṣu pariniṣṭhitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 92, Verse 7
daśabhiś citrasenaṃ ca vikarṇaṃ pañcaviṃśatyā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 92, Verse 8
duryodhanaṃ tribhir viddhvā supuṃkhais tigmatejasaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 92, Verse 10
tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ kurumādhavavīrayoḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 92, Verse 28
prayāhi satvaraṃ sūta rathena rathasattamam nihaniṣyāmi taṃ saṃkhe vṛṣṇivīram ariṃdamam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 92, Verse 35
acalaḥ sa purā bhūtvā samakampata māriṣa

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 92, Verse 36
hatāśvasūte tu rathe sthitāya śinipuṃgavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 92, Verse 37
praiṣayat sātyako bāṇaṃ hārdikyasya nararṣabhaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 92, Verse 38
sahemavikṛtaṃ varma nirbhidya kṛtavarmaṇaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 92, Verse 41
na hi tasya raṇe pārthaḥ kathaṃ cid api bhārata didṛkṣuḥ sa hi vegena prāyād yatra dhanaṃjayaḥ svaśaktyā kṣatriyais tatra niruddho balavattaraḥ yuyudhe sātvato rājan didṛkṣuḥ pāṇḍunandanam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 93, Verse 2
prāvartata mahāraudraḥ saṃgrāmo lomaharṣaṇaḥ śaineyasya ca rājendra bhāradvājasya cobhayoḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 93, Verse 21
mādhavo 'pi mahārāja brāhmaṇaṃ pīḍayann iva

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 93, Verse 29
tataḥ sārathinaṃ hatvā droṇasyāpātayad rathāt śoṇāśvāś ca rathaṃ gṛhya dudruvuḥ sarvatodiśam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 94, Verse 2
hatān nihantāsmi kirīṭamālinā hy ahaṃ sabhīmaḥ saha pārṣatena

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 94, Verse 16
mudā mahatyābhiyuto mahātmā mahāhave śakra ivāmareśaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 1
duryodhanaṃ ca nirjitya śūraṃ caiva sudarśanam jalasaṃdhaṃ nihatyājau śūrasenaṃ ca pārthivam mlecchāṃś ca bahudhā rājan kāśyaputraṃ ca saṃyuge niṣādāṃs taṃkaṇāṃś caiva kaliṃgān magadhān api kekayāñ śūrasenāṃś ca tathā parvatavāsinaḥ kāmbojān yavanāṃś caiva vasātīṃś ca śibīn api kosalān magadhāṃś caiva yātudhānān satittirān etāṃś cānyān raṇe hatvāgacchad yuddhe sa sātyakiḥ rudhiraughanadīṃ ghorāṃ keśaśaivalaśāḍvalām śaktigrāhasamākīrṇāṃ chattrahaṃsopaśobhitām dustarāṃ bhīrubhir nityaṃ śūralokapravāhinīm

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 4
śauryasattvabalopetaṃ śūravāṇijasevitam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 8
dravate tad yathā sainyaṃ tena bhagnaṃ mahātmanā rathair viparidhāvadbhir gajair aśvaiś ca sārathe kauśeyāruṇasaṃkāśam etad uddhūyate rajaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 9
viṣphāryamāṇasya raṇe gāṇḍīvasyāmitaujasaḥ abhyāśastham ahaṃ manye saindhavasya kirīṭinam tādṛśaḥ śrūyate śabdaḥ sainyānāṃ sāgaropamaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 21
pārthivās tasya vividhaṃ mahāstrasya prayojanam makaradhvajān mahāmuṣṭiṃ kṛṣṇād dureṣupātanam jagāda saṃbhramo yuddhe mokṣaḥ śūrātmajātmajaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 23
adya me yuddhyamānasya phalgunasyeva sāyakān patitān rathanāgeṣu dṛṣṭvā śocanti śatravaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 26
rudhirokṣitasarvāṅgān madbāṇaśakalīkṛtān dṛṣṭvā nāgavarān saṃkhye

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 29
balaṃ vīryaṃ kṛtajñatvaṃ mama jñāsyanti kauravāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 30
saindhavāṃś coditā yantrā ūhus te satyakaṃ raṇe tataḥ śaśāṅkasaṃkāśān vikurvāṇān hayottamān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 32
**** **** yavanāḥ sumahābalāḥ kebeti vādinaḥ sarve

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 38
hatair yavanakāmbojaiḥ kirātaiḥ saha barbaraiḥ padātibhiś ca vīreṇa sātvatena hate raṇe patitair abhavan rājan saṃvṛtā raṇabhūmayaḥ evaṃ tad yavanānīkaṃ hatvā chittvā ca mādhavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 42
teṣām astrāṇi bāṇāṃś ca śaineyo nataparvabhiḥ nicakarta mahārāja yavanānāṃ śirodharān te śarā nataparvāṇo yuyudhānena preritāḥ bhittvā dehāṃs tathā teṣāṃ patanti sma mahītale te hanyamānā vīrās tu vṛṣṇivīreṇa saṃyuge śastrāhatāḥ patanty urvyāṃ kāmbojāḥ sapadānugāḥ kāmbojānāṃ bhujaiś chinnaiḥ yavanānāṃ ca bhārata tatra tatra mahī bhāti pañcāsyair iva pannagaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 46
tat tasya samare karma dṛṣṭvānyair akṛtaṃ purā cāraṇāḥ saha gandharvāḥ pūjayāṃ cakrire bhṛśam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 95, Verse 47
na ke cid abhyavartanta tāvakā vṛṣṇinandanam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 96, Verse 17
tūṇīcarmāsimad ghoraṃ gajāśvarathasaṃkulam udvṛttaḥ sāgaro yadvad velām āśrayate tathā mām āsādya hi tiṣṭhanti yaudhāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 96, Verse 20
laghvastraḥ citrayodhī ca prahasañ śinipuṃgavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 96, Verse 21
prāvartata mahārāja devāsuraraṇopamaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 96, Verse 23
sa śarair analasparśair ākarṇād abhicoditaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 96, Verse 24
nāsīn moghaḥ śaraḥ kaś cid āsan sarve tanucchidaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 96, Verse 26
rathinaḥ pattināgāś ca sādinaś ca śarā hatāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 96, Verse 33
śyenavad vyacarat saṃkhye śaineyo laghu suṣṭhu ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 96, Verse 44
taṃ prayāntaṃ mahābāhuṃ tāvakāḥ prekṣya māriṣa dṛṣṭaṃ cādṛṣṭavat kṛtvā kriyām anyāṃ prayojayan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 97, Verse 9
na śakyaḥ samare jetuṃ nihaniṣyati me sutān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 97, Verse 11
śṛṇuṣva rājan saṃgrāmaṃ naravājigajakṣayam duryodhanāpanītena tava durmantritena ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 97, Verse 16
niyutaiś ca padātyaughair vividhāyudhapāṇibhiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 97, Verse 20
saṃprādravan mahat sainyaṃ bhagnaṃ ca bahudhā śaraiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 97, Verse 24
mlecchāsthitair mahārāja bhinnāñjanacayopamaiḥ mṛgair mandaiś ca bhadraiś ca mṛgamandais tathāparaiḥ bhadrair mandamanobhiś ca mṛgabhadrais tathaiva ca mandair mandamadaiś caiva tathā mandamṛgair api tatra tatra dharākīrṇā śayānaiḥ parvatopamaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 97, Verse 25
kumudasya tathā nāgā airāvatakulodbhavāḥ nihatāḥ satyakenājau nārācair agnisaṃnibhaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 97, Verse 31
abhyadravanta śaineyaṃ rājānam iva mantriṇaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 97, Verse 33
śaineyam abhyadhāvaṃs te grāvabhir dṛḍhahastavat mlecchāḥ pipāsavaḥ prājñā rājānam iva mantriṇaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 97, Verse 37
sātvatasya ca bhallena niṣpiṣṭais tais tathādribhiḥ nipatan nihatā mlecchās tatra tatra gatāsavaḥ te hanyamānāḥ samare sātvatena mahātmanā aśmavṛṣṭiṃ mahāghorāṃ pātayanti sma sātvate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 97, Verse 43
aśmanāṃ bhidyamānānāṃ sāyakaiḥ śrūyate dhvaniḥ padmapatreṣu dhārāṇāṃ patantīnām iva dhvaniḥ hatvā pañcaśatān yodhān sa kṣaṇenaiva māriṣa vyacarat pṛtanāmadhye śaineyaḥ kṛtahastavat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 97, Verse 50
āyuṣman vidravaty eva kurūṇāṃ sainyam āturam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 3
dāsī jitāsi dyūte tvaṃ yathākāmacarī bhava vāsasāṃ vāhikā rājño bhrātur jyeṣṭhasya me bhava na santi patayaḥ sarve te 'dya ṣaṇḍhatilaiḥ samāḥ duḥśāsanaivam uktvā tvaṃ pūrvaṃ kasmāt palāyase

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 13
tvarito vīra gaccha tvaṃ gāndhāry udaram āviśa pṛthivyāṃ dhāvamānasya na saṃpaśyāmi te śamam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 18
mayā śamavatā cokto rakṣa śeṣaṃ suyodhana saṃśāmya vīra pārthais tvaṃ rakṣa sarvān mahīkṣitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 28
nanāda balavān nādaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 32
yathā vāyur mahābhrāṇi vivānnityaṃ viyaty uta

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 38
adṛśyaṃ samare cakrur bhāradvājaṃ sudhanvinaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 39
krodham āhārayat teṣām abhāvāya dvijarṣabhaḥ tataḥ śaramayaṃ jālaṃ droṇas teṣām avāsṛjat te hanyamānā droṇasya śarair ākarṇacoditaiḥ kartavyaṃ nābhyajānan vai kumārā rājasattama tān vimūḍhān raṇe droṇaḥ prahasann iva bhārata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 40
nyakṛntac cottamāṅgāni yathā tālavanāni ha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 42
tad asya bhrājate rājan meghamadhye taḍid yathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 50
āsannam āgataṃ dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ jighāṃsayā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 52
kṛtasaṃkalpabhūyiṣṭaḥ prādravat svarathaṃ prati

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 53
droṇaś cāpi mahārāja śarair vivyādha pārṣatam tad adbhutam abhūd yuddhaṃ droṇapāñcālayos tadā trailokyakāṅkṣiṇor āsīc chakraprahrādayor iva maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi yamakānītarāṇi ca carantau yuddhamārgajñau tatakṣatur atheṣubhiḥ mohayantau manāṃsy ājau yodhānāṃ droṇapārṣatau sṛjantau śaravarṣāṇi varṣāsv iva balāhakau chādayantau mahātmānau śarair vyoma diśo mahīm

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 98, Verse 54
kṣatriyā abruvan rājan vainateyo 'yam ity uta

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 99, Verse 1
rathavrātena mahatā nānādeśodbhavena ca sarvato bharataśreṣṭha visṛjan sāyakān bahūn parjanya iva ghoṣeṇa nādayan vai diśo daśa tam āpatantam ālokya sātyakiḥ kauravaṃ raṇe abhidrutya mahābāhuś chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ te chādyamānā bāṇaughair duḥśāsanapurogamāḥ prādravan samare bhītās tava putrasya paśyataḥ teṣu dravatsu rājendra putro duḥśāsanas tava tasthau vyapetabhī rājan sātyakiṃ cārdayac charaiḥ caturbhir vājinas tasya sārathiṃ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ sātyakiṃ ca śatenājau viddhvā nādaṃ mumoca saḥ tataḥ kruddho mahārāja mādhavas tasya saṃyuge rathaṃ sūtaṃ dhvajaṃ taṃ ca cakre 'dṛśyam ajihmagaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 99, Verse 3
tvaran samāvṛṇod bāṇair duḥśāsanam amitrajit

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 99, Verse 13
tatas tān hatavidhvastān kṛtvā yodhān sahasraśaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 99, Verse 21
tato 'sya vāhān niśitaiś caturbhir ahanac charaiḥ sārathiṃ cāsya saṃkruddho rathi* * * * * * *

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 99, Verse 22
preṣayām āsa vīrāya gṛddhrapakṣāñ śilāśitān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 99, Verse 26
taṃ prāptam api neyeṣa hantuṃ duḥśāsanaṃ raṇe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 100, Verse 1
yat kṛtaṃ vṛṣṇivīreṇa karma śaṃsasi me raṇe naitad utsahate kartuṃ karma śakro 'pi saṃjaya aśraddheyam acintyaṃ ca karma tasya mahātmanaḥ vṛṣṇyandhakapravīrasya śrutvā me vyathitaṃ manaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 100, Verse 3
na santi tasmāt putrā me yathā saṃjaya bhāṣase

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 100, Verse 8
uddhṛtā pṛthivī nūnaṃ yuddhahetoḥ samāgataiḥ iti tatra janāḥ smāhur dṛṣṭvā tāṃ janasaṃsadam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 100, Verse 10
tāvakānāṃ tadā hy āsan prayutāny arbudāni ca tathaiva rājan pāṇḍūnāṃ sahasrāṇi sahasraśaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 100, Verse 11
pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca garjatām itaretaram kṣveḍāḥ kilakilāśabdās tatrāsan vai sahasraśaḥ bherīśabdāś ca tumulā bāṇaśabdāś ca bhārata anyonyaṃ nighnatāṃ caiva narāṇāṃ śuśruve svanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 100, Verse 20
dhvajaśastrapratihatā lokān samavadīpayan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 100, Verse 29
tribhis tribhir yamau vīrau dharmarājaṃ ca saptabhiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 100, Verse 33
ajastraṃ maṇḍalībhūtaṃ dadṛśuḥ samare janāḥ tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā bhallābhyām acchinad dhanuḥ tava putrasya kauravya yatamānasya saṃyuge

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 100, Verse 36
tato 'nyad dhanur ādāya tava putraḥ pratāpavān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 100, Verse 38
tathā tava mahat sainyaṃ tad vyarocata tāpayan saṃprahṛṣṭas tu sahasā tava sainyārṇavaṃ prati loḷayan sarvato gatvā samudraṃ makaro yathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 100, Verse 39
tatra sma kadanaṃ ghoraṃ vartate pāṇḍupūrvaja atīva sarvaśabdebhyo lomaharṣakaraḥ prabho arjunasya mahābāho tāvakānāṃ ca dhanvinām madhye bhāratasainyasya mādhavasya mahāraṇe droṇasyāpi paraiḥ sārdhaṃ vyūhadvāre mahāraṇe evam eṣa kṣayo vṛttaḥ pṛthivyāṃ pṛthivīpate kruddhe 'rjune tathā droṇe sātvate ca mahārathe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 3
jaghāna somakān rājan sṛñjayān kekayān api

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 5
bhrātṝṇāṃ pañcamo jyeṣṭhaḥ spardhamāno mahārathaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 9
preṣayat sa śarān aṣṭau sahasraṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 13
brāhmeṇāstreṇa tan muktaṃ brāhmam astraṃ viśāṃ pate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 14
kaikeyo 'straṃ samālokya muktaṃ droṇena saṃyuge brahmāstreṇaiva rājendra brāhmam astram aśātayat tato 'stre nihate brāhme bṛhatkṣatraś ca bhārata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 20
vyasṛjat sarvato bāṇān kekayasya vimohanāt sārathiṃ cāsya bāṇena rathanīḍād apāharat dvābhyāṃ dhvajaṃ ca chattraṃ ca chittvā bhūmāv apātayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 21
tataḥ sādhuvisṛṣṭena nārācena dvijarṣabhaḥ hṛdy avidhyad bṛhatkṣatraṃ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 29
sāratheś ca śiraḥ kāyāc cakarta prahasann iva

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 30
avaplutya rathāc caidyo gadām ādāya satvaraḥ bhāradvājāya cikṣepa ruṣitām iva pannagīm

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 34
tomaraṃ pañcabhiś chittvā śaktiṃ ciccheda saptabhiḥ tau jagmatur mahīṃ chinnau sarpāv iva garutmatā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 36
sa gāḍhaviddhas tenāśu hṛdi rājan mahārathaḥ papāta ca rathāt tūrṇaṃ dhṛṣṭaketur mahāyaśāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 48
pratāpyamānāḥ sūryeṇa hanyamānāś ca sāyakaiḥ anvapadyanta pāñcālās tadā saṃtrastacetasaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 50
bruvantaś ca raṇe 'nyonyaṃ cedipāñcālasṛñjayāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 59
**** **** kṣatradharmā mahābalaḥ krodhasaṃvignamanaso

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 61

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 63

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 101, Verse 65
tam ācāryas tribhir bāṇair bāhvor urasi cārdayat dhvajaṃ saptabhir unmathya yantāram avadhīt tribhiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 26
sa kaśmalasamāviṣṭo bhīmam āhūya pārthivaḥ abravīd vacanaṃ rājan kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 32
yathā hi pāñcajanyasya śrūyate ninado mahān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 36
mama priyahitārthaṃ ca śakralokād ihāgataḥ vṛddhopasevī dhṛtimān kṛtajñaḥ satyasaṃgaraḥ praviṣṭo mahatīṃ senām arpayantāṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ praviṣṭe ca camūṃ ghorām arjune śatrunāśane preṣitaḥ sātvato vīraḥ phalgunasya padānugaḥ tasyābhigamanaṃ jāne bhīma nāvartanaṃ punaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 40
na hi śudhyati me bhāvas tayor evaṃ paraṃtapa

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 51
mayi jīvati kaunteya bhāradvājaḥ kathaṃ cana

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 53
kṛtvā pradakṣiṇān viprān arcitāṃs tuṣṭamānasān ālabhya maṅgalāny aṣṭau pītvā kairātakaṃ madhu dviguṇadraviṇo vīro madaraktāntalocanaḥ vipraiḥ kṛtasvastyayano vijayotpādasūcitaḥ paśyann evātmano buddhiṃ vijayānandakāriṇīm anulomānilaiś cāśu pradarśitajayodayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 54
ratham āruhya niryuktaṃ sarvopakaraṇānvitam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 63
tataḥ pāṇḍusuto rājan bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān baddhagodhāṅgulitrāṇaḥ pragṛhītaśarāsanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 64
talaśabdena vīrāṇāṃ pātayitvā manāṃsy uta

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 67
taṃ samāyāntam ālokya ghorarūpaṃ sutās tava

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 71
taiḥ samantād vṛtaḥ śūraiḥ samare sa mahārathaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 77
tasya droṇo rathaṃ rājañ chādayām āsa saṃyuge sāśvasūtadhvajaṃ tūrṇaṃ tad adbhutam ivābhavat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 79
bhīmaṃ pūjāṃ kariṣyantaṃ guruvṛttam athābravīt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 88
vicacāra raṇe rājan vāyutulyaparākramaḥ droṇaṃ tu virathaṃ kṛtvā bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ abhyavartata sainyāni tāvakāni samantataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 89
bhīmenaivākarod yatnaṃ vyūham evābhyarakṣata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 97
te śarair bhīmakarmāṇaṃ vavarṣuḥ pāṇḍavaṃ yudhi meghā ivātapāpāye dhārābhir dharaṇīdharam sa tad bāṇamayaṃ varṣam aśmavarṣam ivācalaḥ pratīcchan pāṇḍudāyādo na prāvyathata śatruhā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 99
tomareṇa nihatyājau preṣayām āsa mṛtyave

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 100
diśo vidrāvayām āsa nīhāram iva bhāskaraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 102, Verse 105
bhīṣayitvā rathānīkaṃ hatvā yodhān varān varān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 103, Verse 5
prāmathnāt sā mahārāja sainikāṃs tava saṃyuge

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 103, Verse 7
te hanyamānā bhīmena gadāhastena tāvakāḥ prādravanta raṇe bhītā vyāghraghrātā mṛgā iva

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 103, Verse 13
aṃse śiro bhīmasenaḥ karau kṛtvorasi sthirau vegam āsthāya balavān manonilagarutmatām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 103, Verse 16
parāṅmukhaṃ tathā yāntaṃ bhagnotsāhaṃ guruṃ tadā gatvā vegena taṃ bhīmo dhuraṃ gṛhya rathasya tu tam apy atirathaṃ bhīmaś cikṣepa bhṛśaroṣitaḥ evam aṣṭau rathāḥ kṣiptā guror bhīmena līlayā droṇo 'pi tu nimeṣeṇa punaḥ svaratham āsthitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 103, Verse 26
vāsudevaś ca kauravya bhīmasenasya saṃyuge

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 103, Verse 39
kālakeyān maheṣvāsān sahasrāṇi caturdaśa

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 104, Verse 4
aśvam aśvena samare manujair manujāṃs tathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 104, Verse 7
na me 'rjunād bhayaṃ tādṛk kṛṣṇān nāpi ca sātvatāt hutabhug janmano naiva yādṛg bhīmād bhayaṃ mama

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 104, Verse 9
karṇo 'py abhyapatad dhīmāṃs tumulena raveṇa ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 104, Verse 10
rurodha mārgaṃ bhīmasya vātasyeva mahīruhaḥ bhīmo 'pi dṛṣṭvā sāvegaṃ puro vaikartanaṃ sthitam cukopa balavad vīraś cikṣepāsya śilāśitān tān pratyagṛhṇāt karṇo 'pi pratīpaṃ preṣayac charān tatas tu sarvayodhānāṃ yatatāṃ prekṣatāṃ tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 104, Verse 13
keṣāṃ cid alpasattvānāṃ taṃ śrutvā ninadaṃ yudhi śastrāṇi nyapatan dorbhyaḥ keṣāṃ cic cāsavo 'dravan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 104, Verse 14
taṃ śrutvā ninadaṃ ghoraṃ śakṛn mūtraṃ saśoṇitam prasusruvur vāhanāni stabdhāni ca tato 'bhavan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 104, Verse 15
gṛdhrakaṅkabaḍaiś cāsīd antarikṣaṃ samāvṛtam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 104, Verse 23
madhyaṃdinam anuprāptas tritejā iva bhāskaraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 104, Verse 31
cakre yudhiṣṭhiraḥ saṃkhye harṣanādaiś ca saṃkulām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 104, Verse 32
śuśruve bhīmasenasya tad adbhutam ivābhavat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 104, Verse 33
tato vyāyacchamānasya bhīmasenasya saṃyuge tat sainyaṃ kaluṣībhūtaṃ na prājñāyata kiṃ cana

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 105, Verse 2
iha dṛṣṭa ito naṣṭaḥ sarathaḥ prādravan nṛpaḥ muhūrtād iva putras te droṇam āsādya māriṣa

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 105, Verse 3
sasaṃrambham idaṃ vākyam abravīt kurunandanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 105, Verse 4
atikramya ca hatvā ca sainyāni sumahānti ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 105, Verse 7
ity evaṃ bruvate yodhā aśraddheyam idaṃ tava

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 105, Verse 16
na te 'kṣā niśitā ghorāḥ śarā yuṣmat tanucchadaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 105, Verse 18
atra te dhruvam āyatto jayo vājaya eva vā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 105, Verse 24
pārśve bhittvā camūṃ vīrau praviṣṭau tava vāhinīm

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 105, Verse 26
yudhāmanyuś ca pāñcālya uttamaujās tathaiva ca bhittvā pārśvena sainyaṃ tu praviṣṭau phalgunaṃ prati tau samāsādayad vīraḥ śaraiḥ kāyāsthibhedibhiḥ saptabhiś ca yudhāmanyuṃ ṣaḍbhiś caivottamaujasam tau taṃ suniśitair bāṇair avidhyetāṃ mahārathau uttamaujās tu bhallena cāpaṃ ciccheda vīryavān athānyat sumahātejā dhanur gṛhya mahābalaḥ chādayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ pāñcālau kurunandanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 105, Verse 27
tathottamaujāḥ saṃkruddhaḥ śarair hemavibhūṣitaiḥ avidhyat sārathiṃ cāsya prāhiṇod yamasādanam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 105, Verse 29
yudhāmanyurathaṃ śīghram āruroha paraṃtapaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 105, Verse 34
etad īdṛśakaṃ kārṣīt putras tava janādhipa gadayā gadināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ sarvalokamahārathaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 0
saṃjaya uvāca vartamāne mahārāja saṃgrāme lomaharṣaṇe vyākuleṣu ca sainyeṣu pīḍyamāneṣu sarvaśaḥ rādheyo bhīmam ānarcchad yuddhāya bharatarṣabha yathā nāgo vane nāgaṃ matto mattam abhidravat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 5
bhayād yasya mahābāhor na śete bahulāḥ samāḥ cintayan nityaśo vīryaṃ rādheyasya mahātmanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 15
astrahetoḥ purā tāta bhārgavaṃ samapūjayat tasya prasādād brahmāstraṃ labdhavāṃś ca bhṛgūttamāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 19
karṇa uvāca bhīmāhitais tava raṇe svapne 'pi na vibhāvitam tad darśayasi kasmān me pṛṣṭhaṃ pārthadidṛkṣayā kuntyāḥ putrasya sadṛśaṃ nedaṃ pāṇḍavanandana tena mām abhitaḥ sthitvā śaravarṣair avākira

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 35
sa karṇacāpaṃ ciccheda bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ trāsayitvā mahārāja gām amitavikramaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 44
punar bāṇamayaṃ varṣaṃ vyasṛjat pāṇḍavaṃ prati tathā karṇena samare pīḍyamānaḥ samantataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 47
samṛddhakusumāpīḍo vasante 'śokavat taruḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 49
saptabhir niśitais tūrṇaṃ śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 50
marmaṇy anaparādhī saṃdidhitsuḥ kalahaṃ tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 51
tathāpi samare tūrṇaṃ vivyādhorasi pāṇḍavaḥ pāṇḍavas tu punar viddhvā saptabhiḥ sāyakottamaiḥ anyaiś ca bahu saṃ(?)rājañ śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 53
samāśvastas tu karṇo vai punar yuddham arocayat bhīmaseno dṛḍhaṃ kopāt punar vivyādha patriṇā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 106, Verse 54
apacakrāma samare yuddhāya bharatarṣabha bhīmasenabhayāt karṇaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 107, Verse 1
kathaṃ ca yuyudhe bhīmo vīryaślāghī mahābalaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 107, Verse 2
śiṣyatvaṃ prāptavān karṇas tasya tulyo 'stramāyayā tad viśiṣṭo 'pi vā karṇaḥ śiṣyaḥ śiṣyaguṇair yutaḥ kālāntakayamo yadvad bhīmasenena nirjitaḥ kuntīputreṇa bhīmena nirjitaḥ sa tu līlayā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 107, Verse 3
bhīmaseno 'pi samare rādheyaṃ pratyamarṣitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 107, Verse 11
keśapakṣagrahaṃ caiva duḥśāsanakṛtaṃ tathā paruṣāṇi ca vākyāni karṇenoktāni bhārata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 107, Verse 14
putras tava viśeṣeṇa kāladyūtena noditaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 107, Verse 16
evaṃ bahuvidhān ghorān smaran dīptāgnisaṃnibhaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 107, Verse 35
tato bhīmo mahārāja karṇaṃ viddhvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥ sārathiṃ cāsya bhallena rathanīḍād apāharat aśvāṃś ca caturaḥ śvetān nijaghāna śitaiḥ śaraiḥ hitvā dhvajaṃ ca chattraṃ ca rathaṃ ca śatadhākarot cakāra virathaṃ karṇaṃ tava putrasya paśyataḥ sa tathā virathaḥ karṇo bhīmasenena nirjitaḥ anyaṃ rathaṃ samāsthāya punar vivyādha mārutim mahāgajau yathā dṛptau viṣāṇāgraiḥ parasparam tatakṣatus tathā tau tu anyonyaṃ ca nijaghnatuḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 107, Verse 39
ākrīḍam iva rudrasya dakṣayajñanibarhaṇe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 108, Verse 10
karṇasya matam āsthāya svārtham ity eva me sutaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 108, Verse 13
tān utkramyābravīt putro mama dyūte sumandadhīḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 108, Verse 16
hanta te kathayiṣyāmi tayoḥ prāṇada(?du)rodaram paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ keśavārjunayor api

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 108, Verse 22
śaktiṃ viyadgatāṃ drṣṭvā śakrāśanisamadyutim

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 108, Verse 27
suvarṇavikṛtair bāṇaiḥ suvarṇavikṛtāñ śarān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 108, Verse 33
sārathiṃ ca tathāpy asya rathanīḍād apātayat tato vaikartanaḥ karṇaś cintāṃ prāpa duratyayām sa chādyamānaḥ samare hatāśvo hatasārathiḥ mohitaḥ śarajālena kartavyaṃ nābhyapadyata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 109, Verse 7
ciccheda kārmukaṃ tūrṇaṃ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 109, Verse 9
tato bhīmo mahābāhuḥ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 109, Verse 12
mahābalān mahāvegān sadaśvān gadayā hatān sūtaṃ ca nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā ketuṃ ca vinipātitam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 109, Verse 27
te medinīṃ prasarpantaḥ śobhante rudhirokṣitāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 109, Verse 33
tathā puruṣamānī san pratyapāyād raṇājirāt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 110, Verse 6
pataṃgam iva saṃdīptaṃ bhīmāgniṃ samaveśayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 110, Verse 19
sa nūnaṃ nirjitaṃ karṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmena saṃyuge

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 110, Verse 23
aho mama sutānāṃ hi vipannaṃ sūta jīvitam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 110, Verse 26
sukṛtasya supṛṣṭasya sujātasya mahāmṛdhe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 110, Verse 35
bhīmasenas tato bāṇaiḥ pañca rājan sutāṃs tava

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 111, Verse 2
nicakhāna sa saṃbhrāntaḥ pūrvavairam anusmaran

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 111, Verse 5
raṇe bhūyo 'pi rādheyaṃ viddhvā pañcabhir āyasaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 111, Verse 8
papātātha mahac cāpaṃ hemapṛṣṭhaṃ durāsadam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 111, Verse 15
sa chādyamāno bāṇaughair bhīmasenadhanuścyutaiḥ punar evābhavat karṇo bhīmasenāt parāṅmukhaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 111, Verse 19
tān āpatata evāśu bhīmaseno mahārathaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 111, Verse 23
sūtaputro 'pi kaunteyaṃ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ pañcāśatā mahābāhur vivyādha bharatarṣabha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 111, Verse 25
krodhāgnitejasā dīptau saṃrambhād raktalocanau vyabhrājetāṃ mahārāja vidhūmāv iva pāvakau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 111, Verse 26
śaradhārāsṛjau vīrau meghāv iva vavarṣatuḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 111, Verse 29
vāraṇāv iva cānyonyaṃ viṣāṇābhyām ariṃdamau nirbhindantau svagātrāṇi sāyakaiś cāru rejatuḥ nādayantau pravalgantau vikrīḍantau parasparam maṇḍalāni vikurvāṇau rathābhyāṃ rathasattamau vṛṣabhāv iva nardantau balinau vāsitāntare siṃhāv iva parākrāntau narasiṃhau mahābalau parasparaṃ vīkṣamāṇau krodhasaṃraktalocanau yuyudhāte mahāvīryau śakravairocanī yathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 111, Verse 32
bhīmam ācchādayat tūrṇaṃ yathādriṃ toyado 'mbunā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 112, Verse 2
putrāṃs tava dadarśātha bhīmasenena pātitān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 112, Verse 25
nirāsata sa dehebhyaḥ putrāṇām atha tair asūn

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 112, Verse 27
hitvā hitvā kṣitiṃ jagmus teṣām evāsubhiḥ saha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 112, Verse 30
saṃjaya uvāca agādhabuddhir gāṅgeyaḥ kṣitau suraguroḥ samaḥ tyājitaḥ samare prāṇān ajeyas tridaśair api yuddhadharme na saṃbandhā bhavanti kurusattama vikarṇa tenāsi hataḥ pratijñā rakṣitā mayā tvam agāḥ saṃgaraṃ vīra kṣātradharmam anusmaran viśeṣato 'si nṛpates tathāsmākaṃ hite rataḥ nyāyato 'nyāyato naivam ekaḥ śoko mahādyutiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 112, Verse 32
ācaṣṭeva ca tad yuddhaṃ bhīmasya vijayaṃ tathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 112, Verse 38
sabhām ānāyya pāñcālīṃ karṇena sahito 'lpadhīḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 112, Verse 39
śṛṇvatas tava rājendra kauravāṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 112, Verse 41
yac ca ṣaṇḍhatilādīni paruṣāṇi tavātmajaiḥ śrāvitās te mahātmānaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kopayiṣṇubhiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 112, Verse 43
tvayā vṛddhena dhīreṇa kāryatattvārthadarśinā na kṛtaṃ suhṛdāṃ vākyaṃ daivam atra parāyaṇam tan mā śuco naravyāghra tavaivāpanayo mahān vināśahetuḥ putrāṇāṃ bhavān eva mato mama

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 113, Verse 17
śatakumbhavicitraiś ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 113, Verse 21
valayair apaviddhaiś ca tathaivāṅguliveṣṭanaiḥ cūḍāmaṇibhir uṣṇīṣaiḥ svarṇasūtraiś ca māriṣa

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 113, Verse 26
meghajālanibhaṃ sainyam āsīt tava narādhipa

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 1
punaś caturbhis tīkṣṇāgrair avidhyat kaṅkapatribhiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 3
vivyādha subhṛśaṃ saṃkhye tailadhautena māriṣa

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 4
gāṅgeyapulinān mattaś cakravāko nadann iva maṇimāṇikyajaḍitaṃ hutabhuk tigmatejasam nigalad amṛtād ekāt tāmarasaṃ suraśilpinā kṛtam śravaṇakuṇḍalaṃ karṇamadhyato nyapatad athāsya śuddham uttamam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 8
so 'tividdho bhṛśaṃ karṇaḥ pāṇḍavena tarasvinā rathakūbaram ālambya nyamīlayata locane sa muhūrtāt punaḥ saṃjñāṃ labdhvā karṇaḥ paraṃtapaḥ rudhirokṣitasarvāṅgaḥ krodham āhārayat param

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 11
tān acintya mahābāhur bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 12
śaradaṃṣṭrau samāsādya tatakṣatur anantaram

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 16
tadapy atha nimeṣārdhāc cicchedāsya vṛkodaraḥ tṛtīyaṃ ca caturthaṃ ca pañcamaṃ ṣaṣṭham eva ca saptamaṃ cāṣṭamaṃ caiva navamaṃ daśamaṃ tathā ekādaśaṃ dvādaśaṃ ca trayodaśam athāpi vā caturdaśaṃ pañcadaśaṃ ṣoḍaśaṃ ca vṛkodaraḥ tathā saptadaśaṃ caivam aṣṭādaśam athāpi vā bahūni bhīmaś ciccheda karṇasyaivaṃ dhanūṃṣi ca nimeṣārdhāt tataḥ karṇo dhanurhasto vyatiṣṭhata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 17
rathair vimathitair bhagnair aśvaiś cānyaiḥ pravegitaiḥ bhraṣṭaśrīkair naravaraiḥ pāṃsukuṇṭhitamūrdhajaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 39
anyonyaśarasaṃsparśāt tayor manujasiṃhayoḥ ākāśe bharataśreṣṭha pāvakaḥ samajāyata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 53
vyāyacchat sa śarān karṇaḥ kuntīputrajighāṃsayā sahasraśo mahārāja rukmapuṅkhān sutejanān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 54
sa vadhyamāno balavān karṇacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 62
śarair bhīmam atikramya karṇo bhṛśam apīḍayat vidhanvā virathaś caiva vicarmā nirasis tataḥ amṛṣyamāṇaś ca bhṛśaṃ śāntaḥ karṇāstrapīḍitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 64
mahauṣadhisamāyuktaṃ hanūmān iva parvatam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 65
rathāyutāni cikṣepa hayānām ayutāni ca narāyutāni ca tathā karṇāyāmitatejase śaktyṛṣṭiprāsaparighakampanākuṭamudgarān cikṣepa karṇāya balī gṛhītvā medinītalāt tān kṣiptān bhīmabalavad vāyunā samudīrayan raṇāṅgaṇābhyāsagataś cicchedāśu vṛṣas tadā mahāgraha ivāviṣṭo nirviṣaṇṇo vṛkodaraḥ abhyadhāvata rādheyaṃ mūrtimān anilaḥ svayam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 67
bhīmo 'pi muṣṭim udyamya vajragarbhaṃ sudāruṇam hantum aicchat sūtaputraṃ saṃsmarann arjunaṃ kṣaṇāt śakto 'pi nāvadhīt karṇaṃ samarthaḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥ rakṣamāṇaḥ pratijñāṃ tāṃ yā kṛtā savyasācinā tam evaṃ vyākulaṃ bhīmaṃ bhūyo bhūyaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ mūrcchayābhiparītāṅgam akarot sūtanandanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 68
dhanuṣā spṛṣṭamātreṇa kruddhaḥ sarpa iva śvasan ācchidya sa dhanus tasya karṇaṃ mūrdhany atāḍayat tāḍito bhīmasenena krodhād āraktalocanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 72
sūdaṃ tvām aham ājāne mātsyapreṣyakakārakam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 75
saṃjayaḥ evaṃ taṃ virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā smṛtvā karṇo 'bravīd vacaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 76
bhīmasena uvāca evaṃ taṃ virathīkṛtya uccaiḥ saṃtarjya pāṇḍavam mudā paramayā yukto darśayan kṛṣṇapāṇḍavau yuṣmābhir yady ahaṃ mārgyas tadā kiṃ bahujalpitaiḥ atha tvayā na mārgyo 'haṃ tadā gacchāmi muñca mām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 79
bhīmo 'pi rathināṃ śreṣṭho dhanadāc chāpam āptavān gataḥ padmāpahāreṇa praṇāmaṃ nākarot purā anena kāraṇenaiva karṇād bhayam avāptavān karṇenāpi tadotsṛṣṭo mātur vacanakāriṇā mallayuddhaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ kuru duṣkulasaṃbhava mahābalo mahābhogī kīcako nihato yathā tathā tvāṃ ghātayiṣyāmi paśyatsu sarvarājasu bhīmasya matam ājñāya karṇo buddhimatāṃ varaḥ virarāma raṇāt tasmāt paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvinām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 80
karṇena virathīkṛtya tarjyamānaṃ vṛkodaram dṛṣṭvārjuno bhṛśaṃ kruddhaḥ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ tasya kārmukam ārujya babhañjāśu parākramī tato dṛṣṭvā mahārāja vāsudevo mahādyutiḥ arjunārjuna paśyemaṃ bhīmaṃ karṇena bādhitam evam uktas tadā pārthaḥ keśavena mahātmanā bhīmasenaṃ tathābhūtaṃ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ amarṣavaśam āpanno nirdahann iva cakṣuṣā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 85
so 'vaplutya drutaṃ sūto yuyudhānarathaṃ yayau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 114, Verse 89
taṃ parīpsan mahārāja satyajit pārtham abhyayāt śareṇaikena vivyātha taṃ rājānaṃ mahābalaḥ karṇe pārthena vikṣiptaṃ nārācaṃ drauṇir acchinat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 115, Verse 1
dātavyam adya manye 'haṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ svakaṃ punaḥ na vigraho hi balinā śreyase syād yathātathā pādayoḥ praṇatenāpi bhuktvāpy ucchiṣṭam apy areḥ ato 'nyad vāpi kṛtvaiva jīvyaṃ loke nareṇa vai jīvataiva paro lokaḥ sādhyate caiva sarvathā ajīvatas tathaivāsīn na sukhaṃ na parā gatiḥ vināśe sarvathotpanne na bālo budhyate kriyām mithyābhimānadagdho hi na budhyeta kṛtākṛte

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 115, Verse 6
kruddhasya devarājasya śakrasyeva mahādyuteḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 115, Verse 24
tato 'rjuno harṣam avāpa saṃkhye kṛṣṇaś ca dṛṣṭvā puruṣapravīram

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 116, Verse 5
athainam anuvṛttās tu trigartāḥ sahitāḥ punaḥ tīvreṇa rathavaṃśena mahatā paryavārayan vikarṣanto 'timātrāṇi cāpāni bharatarṣabha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 116, Verse 7
punar madhyagato vīra āhave yuddhadurmadaḥ ekaḥ paryacarad raṅge bahudhā sa mahārathaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 116, Verse 8
tāṃ ca senām atikramya trigartānāṃ nararṣabhaḥ ajayac chūrasenāṃś ca yatamānān mahāraṇe ekas tato mahābāhuḥ sahasrāñ śatrutāpanaḥ saṃnaddhānāṃ padātīnām avadhīt puruṣarṣabhaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 116, Verse 11
tair vārito mahārāja satyakaḥ pratyavārayat jaghāna subahūn yaudhāñ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ te hatā nipatanti sma pramṛṣṭā dīrghabāhunā tataḥ prāyād asaṃbhrānto dadarśa ca dhanaṃjayam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 116, Verse 20
priyaśiṣyaś ca te pārtha tvayā tulyaparākramaḥ vidārya kauravīṃ senām eṣa āyāti satyakaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 116, Verse 25
iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā keśavasyārjunas tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 116, Verse 32
bhūriśravāḥ kṛtāstraś ca rakṣyo mādhava satyakaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 116, Verse 36
āmiṣārthī yathā śyeno nityaṃ tiṣṭhati brāhmaṇaḥ grahaṇe dharmaputrasya kaś cit kṣemī bhaven nṛpaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 14
nāhaṃ bhīṣayituṃ śakyo vāṅmātreṇa tu kevalam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 21
tāv ubhau śaravarṣābhyām anyonyam abhivarṣatām bhūriśravāḥ sātyakiś ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 23
daśabhiḥ satyako 'vidhyat saumadattim athāśugaiḥ saumadattiḥ śarān asyañ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 30
vṛṣṭiṃ tām abhivarṣantau śarāṇāṃ mahatīṃ tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 31
bhūyo bhūyaḥ śarai rājaṃs takṣantau krodhamūrcchitau ayudhyetāṃ mahāraṅge vane kesariṇāv iva marmajñāv iva saṃkruddhau jighāṃsantau jagarjatuḥ vimardantāv athānyonyaṃ balavajradharāv iva athānyonyaṃ patākāś ca rathopakaraṇāni ca saṃcicchedatur āyastau bāṇaiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ punaś ca śaravarṣābhyām anyonyam abhivarṣatām ubhau ca jaghnatus tūrṇam itaretarasārathī

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 35
bhrāntam udbhrāntam āviddham āplutaṃ viplutaṃ drutam saṃpātaṃ samudīrṇaṃ ca darśayantau yaśasvinau asibhyāṃ saṃprajahrāte parasparam ariṃdamau ubhau chidraiṣiṇau vīrāv ubhau citraṃ vavalgatuḥ darśayantāv ubhau śikṣāṃ lāghavaṃ sauṣṭhavaṃ tathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 41
dvātriṃśat karaṇāni syur yāni yuddhāni bhārata tāny adarśayatāṃ tatra yudhyamānau mahābalau pādodaravibandhaiś ca bhūmāv udbhramaṇais tathā gatapratyāgatākṣepaiḥ pātanotthānasaṃplutaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 42
saṃjaya uvāca sindhurājavadhe saktaṃ pārthaṃ kṛṣṇo 'bravīt punaḥ sīdantaṃ sātyakiṃ paśya pārthainaṃ parirakṣa ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 43
dhārtarāṣṭrāś ca ye mukhyā ye ca mukhyā mahārathāḥ nihatā vṛṣṇivīreṇa śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 45
tato jaladanirghoṣaḥ samīpe nṛpasattama

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 47
bahubhir yas tu senābhir durjayaḥ samare 'nagha

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 51
pātite tv atha śaineye kṛṣṇo 'rjunam abhāṣata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 52
arjuna uvāca mām eva ca mahābāho pariyānti mahārathāḥ yathāśakti yatante māṃ yodhayanto janārdana dhruvaṃ ca yodhayāmy etāñ chidrānveṣaṇatatparān rakṣāmi sātyakiṃ caiva saumadattiṃ vaśaṃ gatam aprāpto na mayā kṛṣṇa hantuṃ bhūriśravā raṇe anyena tu samāsaktaṃ mano notsahate mama avaśyaṃ ca mayā kṛṣṇa vṛṣṇivīrasya rakṣaṇam madarthaṃ yudhyamānasya kāryaṃ prāṇair api prabho adharmo vāstu dharmo vā mama mādhava mādhavaḥ pareṇa nihato mā sma prāṇān hāsīn mahārathaḥ evam uktvārjunaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ parān āśu śitaiḥ śaraiḥ chādayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ pare cāpi dhanaṃjayam evaṃ sma yudhyate vīraḥ sātyakiṃ ca muhur muhuḥ prekṣate sma naravyāghro bhūriśravasam eva ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 53
hāhākṛtam abhūt sarvaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahad balam tāvakāś ca mudā yuktāḥ siṃhanādaṃ vicukruśuḥ nimīlitākṣās tv abhavañ janāḥ saṃgrāmabhīravaḥ tathā bhūriśravogras te sātvate naṣṭavikrame

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 56
bahubhir mahārathair eṣa parākrāntair yuyutsubhiḥ yuddhvā bhṛśaṃ pariśrāntaḥ kṣīṇāyudhaparicchadaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 60
ayudhyatāribhir vīras taṃ sma saṃprekṣate muhuḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 61
mama śiṣyo mamārthāya yudhyate mama śatrubhiḥ taṃ kṛṣṇa mokṣayiṣyāmi dāvāt siṃhaśiśuṃ yathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 117, Verse 62
tataḥ kṣurapraṃ niśitaṃ gāṇḍīve samayojayat pārthabāhuvisṛṣṭaḥ sa maholkeva nabhaścyutā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 1
yantramukto mahendrasya dhvajo vṛttotsavo yathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 3
sa vibāhur mahārāja ekapakṣa ivāṇḍajaḥ ekacakro ratho yadvad dharaṇīm āsthito nṛpaḥ uvāca pāṇḍavaṃ caiva sarvakṣatrasya paśyataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 4
**** **** vyāsaktasya ca sātvate anāgaso 'nyamanaso

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 12
vārṣṇeyāpasadaṃ prāpya kṣudraṃ kṛtam idaṃ tvayā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 16
dhanaṃjayena vīreṇa viniḥśvasya muhur muhuḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 19
garhayām āsur apy etau śaśaṃsur bhūridakṣiṇam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 25
acchinaṃ yad ahaṃ bāhuṃ tatra garhyaṃ kim asti ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 26
nābhimanyor vadhaṃ yūyaṃ garhayadhvaṃ kutas tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 30
saṃjaya uvāca dhanaṃjaye bruvaty evaṃ ghṛṇayā ca pariplute avāṅmukhā babhūvuś ca sainikāḥ sarva eva te muhūrtād iva viśramya sātyakiḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥ amarṣavaśam āpannaḥ saumadattinirākṛtaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 32
nivāryamāṇaḥ kṛṣṇena phalgunena ca māriṣa prāyopaviṣṭasya sataḥ pārthac chinnabhujasya ca nṛśaṃsaṃ kṛtavān pāpo yuyudhāno narādhipa

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 36
satyakaḥ kurumukhyasya cicchedaiva śiras tataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 41
martavyam eva sarveṇa caramaṃ pūrvam eva vā manyadhvaṃ mṛta ity eva mā bhūd vo buddhilāghavam tasmin hate mahābāhau yūpaketau mahātmani dhig enam iti cākrandan kṣatriyāḥ krodhamūrcchitāḥ anyena yuktam ity eva bhavitavyaṃ tatheti ca ke cid āsan vimanasaḥ ke cid duḥkhasamanvitāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 44
śṛṇudhvaṃ sarvam eveha śrutvā garhatha mānavāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 48
anuṣṭhitaṃ mayā tac ca tasmād garhatha mūḍhavat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 50
mantraiḥ pūtasya sumahatsv adhareṣu yaśasvinaḥ bhūriśravasa (sic) tasyāśu naivāraṇyagatasya ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 118, Verse 51
dṛṣṭvā sunāsaṃ sukapolayuktaṃ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 119, Verse 1
yaś caivotsahate jetuṃ samastaṃ māmakaṃ balam vistareṇa mamācakṣva sarvam eva tu saṃjaya

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 119, Verse 3
brahyaṇas tv abhavat putro mānaso 'trir mahātapāḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 119, Verse 4
yadur nāma mahārāja sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 119, Verse 11
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā nīyamānāṃ tu vasudevāya devakīm

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 119, Verse 18
nātihṛṣṭamanāḥ so 'pi puram āgān mahīpatiḥ sa pūrvam eva tapasā mām ārādhya jagattraye kasyāpy ajayyas tan mattaḥ prāptavān varam uttamam tathāpy ayaṃ prayāsas tu niṣphalo na bhaviṣyati tasya pautraṃ tu samare tvatputro mohayiṣyati na tu mārayituṃ śakyaḥ kṛṣṇasaṃrakṣito hy asau aham eva ca kṛṣṇo 'smi nāvayor antaraṃ kva cit

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 119, Verse 19
paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ padā cainam atāḍayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 119, Verse 27
śiner duhitṛsaṃbhūta eṣa vīraḥ sa sātyakiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 120, Verse 3
śrūyate puṇḍarīkākṣa triṣu dharmeṣu vartate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 120, Verse 5
saṃjaya uvāca jayadrathavadhe prāpte tāv ubhau kurupāṇḍavau sasmitau samudekṣetāṃ prauḍhā bālā vadhūr iva

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 120, Verse 10
uvāca rājan putras te karṇaṃ rājā suyodhanaḥ satyakaṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca yattau tau darśayann iva

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 120, Verse 22
drauṇinā tvaṃ hi sahito madreśena kṛpeṇa ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 120, Verse 26
tad yathā prayatiṣye 'haṃ paraṃ śaktyā suyodhana

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 120, Verse 28
saindhavārthe paraṃ yatnaṃ kariṣyāmy adya saṃyuge tvatpriyārthaṃ mahārāja jayo daive pratiṣṭhitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 120, Verse 56
nivārya tāñ śaravrātair divyāny astrāṇi darśayan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 120, Verse 68
**** **** narasiṃho mahārathaḥ vavarṣa sāyakais tīkṣṇair vyadhamat sāyakaiḥ pārthaḥ śalabhān iva mārutaḥ chādayām āsa ca tadā sāyakair arjuno raṇe paśyatāṃ sarvayodhānāṃ darśayan pāṇilāghavam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 120, Verse 78
āvavre 'rjunamārgaṃ ca śarajālena bhārata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 120, Verse 88
tato yugāntābhrasamasvanaṃ mahan mahendracāpapratimaṃ sa gāṇḍivam cakarṣa dorbhyāṃ vihasan bhṛśaṃ yayau dahaṃs tvadīyān yamarāṣṭravardhanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 1
ādadānaṃ mahārāja saṃdadhānaṃ ca pāṇḍavam utkarṣantaṃ vikarṣantaṃ nābhyapaśyāma lāghavāt śakrāśanisphoṭasamaṃ sughoraṃ vikṛṣyamāṇasya dhanaṃjayena trāsodvignaṃ bhayodbhrāntaṃ tvadīyaṃ tad balaṃ nṛpa yugāntavātasaṃkṣubdhaṃ caladvīcitaraṅgitam pralīnamīnamakaraṃ sāgarāmbha ivābhavat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 3
ākāśe samadṛśyanta haṃsānām iva paṅktayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 12
bhūyaś caivārjunaṃ saṃkhye śaravarṣair avākirat punaḥ pārthaṃ dhvajaṃ pārthaṃ kirīṭaṃ vājino dhanuḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 14
anastamita āditya etān nirjitya saindhavaḥ na śakyo hantum ity evaṃ manyamāno janārdanaḥ sasmāra cakraṃ daityārir hariś cakraṃ sudarśanam tadādideśa bhagavān smṛtamātram upasthitam astaṃ gatam ivādityaṃ tamasā chādayeti vai tat tathoktaṃ bhagavatā tamo bhūtvā viśāṃ pate andhaṃ tama ivājñānam ādityasyāharat prabhām tato 'sya vismayaḥ pārtha harṣaś caiva bhaviṣyati ātmajīvitalābhāc ca pratijñāyāś ca nāśanāt astaṃgatam ivādityaṃ dṛṣṭvā mohena bāliśaḥ na hi śakṣyaty athātmānaṃ rakṣituṃ harṣasaṃbhavāt etasminn eva kāle tu prahartavyaṃ dhanaṃjaya jayadrathasya kṣudrasya savitur darśanārthinaḥ ity uktvā tu tataḥ pārthaṃ kṣipram evāharat prabhām pārthas tu balavāñ jñātvā tamo dṛṣṭvātiduḥkhitaḥ janārdanena sṛṣṭaṃ vai tama ādityanāśanam abhavaṃs tāvakā dṛṣṭvā harṣasaṃkulacetasaḥ unnamayya śirogrīvam apaśyat saindhavo ravim athārjunaṃ hṛṣīkeśaḥ śokapūrṇam athābravīt paśya kaunteya sindhūnāṃ pārthivaṃ pāpakāriṇam eṣa tiṣṭhati madhye vai syandanasya dhanaṃjaya unnamayya śirogrīvaṃ vīkṣate sūryamaṇḍalam tasya śīghraṃ pṛṣatkena kāyāc chīrṣam apāhara keśavenaivam uktaḥ sann amarṣād raktalocanaḥ udbabarha śaraṃ tīkṣṇam amarair api duḥsaham

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 29
astrasyāsya prabhāveṇa paśubhartuḥ kathaṃ cana yathaitat saindhavaśiraḥ śarair eva dhanaṃjaya vṛddhakṣatre pataty eva tathā nītir vidhīyatām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 30
arjunas tvarayā yuktas tad astraṃ samupāśritaḥ vṛddhakṣatrāśramadvāram aharat tadareḥ śiraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 31
tato dhanaṃjayaḥ śīghraṃ śaraṃ taṃ bhāskaratviṣam ujjihīrṣuḥ śiraḥ kāyāt saindhavasya mahātmanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 32
prapatiṣyati śīrṣe tu kṛṣṇo 'rjunam athābravīt pārtha pārtha śiro hy etad yathā neyān mahītalam tathā kuru kuruśreṣṭha vakṣye tasyāpi kāraṇam śrutvā tu vacanaṃ tasya tvaramāṇo 'stramāyayā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 33
tiryag ūrdhvam adhaś caiva punar ūrdhvam athāpi ca dīrghakālam avāk caiva saṃprakrīḍann ivārjunaḥ tat sainyaṃ sarvato 'paśyan mahad āścaryam adbhutam prāpayat sa śiro yasmād yodhayann eva pārthivān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 34
jayadrathasyārjunabāṇanālaṃ mukhāravindaṃ rudhirāmbusiktam dṛṣṭaṃ naraiś copari vartamānaṃ vidyādharotsṛṣṭam ivaikapadmam sa devaśatrūn iva devarājaḥ kirīṭamālī vyadhamat sapatnān yathā tamāṃsy abhyuditas tamoghnaḥ pūrṇāṃ pratijñāṃ samavāpya dhīraḥ athābravīt keśavaṃ pāṇḍaveyaḥ kiyantam adhvānam idaṃ harāmi kimartham etan na nipātyam urvyāṃ kva ca prayātavyam idaṃ ca śaṃsa śaknomy ahaṃ yatra bhavān bravīti taṃ bhūmideśaṃ ca śiro vinetum

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 39
tac chiraḥ śatadhā rājan papāta pṛthivītale

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 41
tasmiṃs tu nihate vīre saindhave lokaviśrute praharṣam atulaṃ lebhe kṛṣṇaḥ pārthaś ca bhārata kathaṃ tasya jayo na syād iti bhūtāni menire etadarthaṃ śiras tasya cyāvayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ syamantapañcakād bāhyaṃ śarair eva yathākramam kṛtvā tac ca mahat karma nihatya ca jayadratham astraṃ pāśupataṃ pārthaḥ saṃhartum upacakrame saṃharaty api kaunteye tad astraṃ tatra bhārata vavau śītaḥ sugandhaś ca pavano hlādayann iva saṃhāraṃ ca pramokṣaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā tatra divaukasaḥ vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmuḥ praśaśaṃsuś ca pāṇḍavam evam astreṇa tān vīro yodhayitvā dhanaṃjayaḥ jayadrathaśiraḥ paścāc cyāvayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ tac chiraś cyāvamānaṃ tu dadṛśus tāvakā yudhi śalyakarṇakṛpā rājan mohitāḥ savyasācinā śirasi cyāvite tasya śarair āśīviṣopamaiḥ paścāt kāyo 'patad bhūmiṃ śocayan sarvapārthivān dṛṣṭvā tu nihataṃ saṃkhe sindhurājaṃ mahāratham

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 42
bhīmaś ca vṛṣṇisiṃhaś ca yudhāmanyuś ca bhārata uttamaujāś ca vikrāntaḥ śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ pṛthak pṛthak

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 44
udapadyata sainyasya pāṇḍūnāṃ hṛṣṭacetasām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 121, Verse 49
vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca etat sucaritaṃ rājan yaḥ śṛṇotīha bhaktitaḥ apamṛtyuṃ jayaty āśu labhate sarvasaṃpadaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 1
paśyatāṃ sarvayodhānāṃ māmakānāṃ mahāraṇe ahanyata kathaṃ yuddhe saindhavaḥ savyasācinā kathaṃ drauṇikṛpair guptaḥ karṇena ca mahāraṇe phalgunāgnimukhaṃ ghoraṃ praviṣṭaḥ sādhu saindhavaḥ tasmin hate maheṣvāse mandātmā sa suyodhanaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sūta kim akārṣīd anantaram

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 12
aśrupūrṇamukho dīno vacanaṃ cedam abravīt

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 19
putraśokābhibhūtena śarair abhyarditena ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 27
tam āpatantaṃ rādheyam arjunasya rathaṃ prati pāñcālyau sātyakiś caiva sahasā samupādravan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 34
tadā gantāsi pārtha tvaṃ tena yoddhuṃ durātmanā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 35
saumadattiṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā tad yuddham abhavat katham

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 37
paśyatāṃ sarvasainyānāṃ keśavārjunayor api

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 40
ubhayoḥ senayoś caiva ye yaudhāḥ santi ke cana

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 54
karṇas tv amitavikrāntas tava priyahite rataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 56
jalasaṃdhaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā bhūriśravasam eva ca

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 57
abhyardayan mahābāhuḥ sarvakṣatrasya paśyataḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 58
śarair eva prajagrāha satyako vṛṣṇipuṃgavaḥ tatrāścaryaṃ tadā rājann akaroc chininandanaḥ karṇaṃ ca prativivyādha śarāṃs tatprahitāñ śitān tatas tau spardhayā vīrāv ubhau yuddhaviśāradau atakṣatām athānyonyaṃ ubhau vijayakāṅkṣiṇau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 59
bāṇasaṃkulayuddhaiś ca spardhinau yuddhadurmadau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 62
dhvajaṃ ciccheda chattraṃ ca rathaṃ ca śatadhākarot

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 63

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 65
tadā puruṣavīreṇa satyakena tathākṛte

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 71
satyakas tu sutāṃs te vai vyadhamal līlayā śaraiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 73
jitavān sarvasainyāni tāvakāni hasann iva

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 74
pārthena sadṛśo yuddhe vāsudevasamo yuvā sarvakṣatriyavīrāṇāṃ ekavīras tu sūtajam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 122, Verse 76
saṃjayācakṣva bhūyo me yac cakrāte punaś ca tau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 123, Verse 1
kiṃ vai bhīmārjunau tatra sātyakiś cākarot tadā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 123, Verse 7
vacanaṃ bhīmasenasya śrutvā tv amaravikramaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 123, Verse 9
raṇam utsṛjya nirlajja gacchase vai punaḥ punaḥ māhātmyaṃ paśya bhīmasya karṇa janma kule tathā noktavān paruṣaṃ yat tvā palāyanaparāyaṇam bhūyas tvam api saṃgamya sakṛd eva yadṛcchayā virathaṃ hatavān vīraṃ pāṇḍavaṃ sūtadāyada kulasya sadṛśaṃ cāpi rādheya kṛtavān asi tvam idānīṃ naraśreṣṭha prastutaṃ nāvabudhyase sṛgāla iva manye 'haṃ kṣatraṃ tvam avamanyase pitryaṃ karmāsya saṃgrāmas tavāstv anyaḥ kulocitaḥ ahaṃ tvām api rādheya bravīmi raṇamūrdhani sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ madhye kuru kāryāṇi sarvaśaḥ naikāntasiddhiḥ saṃgrāme vāsavasyāpi vidyate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 123, Verse 10
sa tvayā bhīmasenasya jayaḥ prāpto yadṛcchayā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 123, Verse 11
nāriṃ jitvātikatthante na ca jalpanti durvacaḥ na ca kaṃ cana nindanti santaḥ śūrā nararṣabhāḥ tvaṃ tu prākṛtavijñānas tat tad vadasi sūtaja bahvabaddham akarṇyaṃ ca cāpalād aparīkṣitam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 123, Verse 16
ye ca tatrāpi hantāram upayāsyanti māṃ yudhi

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 123, Verse 17
muṇḍinaṃ tu haniṣyāmi tvāṃ ca karṇātimāninam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 123, Verse 19
lohitāyati cāditye tvaramāṇo dhanaṃjayaḥ sahitaś cakrarakṣābhyāṃ śinīnām ṛṣabheṇa ca yudhāmanyurathasthena bhīmena sahito 'nagha jayadrathānugair vīrair yuddhāya samupāyayau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 123, Verse 41
sātyakiḥ pārtham abhyāyād bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ yudhāmanyūttamaujau ca pāñcālasyātmajāv ubhau te nivārya śarair drauṇiṃ karṇaṃ ca saha bhūmipaiḥ agacchan rathinaś caiva yatra rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 124, Verse 1
avatīrya rathād rājā paryaṣvajata keśavam saṃprahṛṣṭamanā rājan dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ diṣṭyā vardhasi rājendra hataśatrur narottama diṣṭyā nistīrṇavāṃś caiva pratijñām anujas tava sa tv evam uktaḥ kṛṣṇena hṛṣṭaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 124, Verse 7
tvatprasādād dhṛṣīkeśa rājyaṃ prāpsyāmi cottamam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 124, Verse 14
purāṇaṃ paramaṃ devaṃ devadevaṃ sanātanam ye prapannāḥ suraguruṃ na te muhyanti karhi cit

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 124, Verse 16
goptāraṃ sarvalokānāṃ yat tad brahma sanātanam lokādiṃ viśvakarmāṇam akṣayakṣaram akṣaram manasaḥ paramāṃ yoniṃ khaṃ vāyur jyotiṣāṃ nidhim

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 124, Verse 17
parameśa pareśeśa tiryag īśa nareśvara sarveśvareśvareśeśa namas te puruṣottama tvam īśeśeśvareśāna prabho vardhasva mādhava prabhavāpyaya sarvasya sarvātman pṛthulocana

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 124, Verse 26
śrībhagavān uvāca evam etan mahābāho vinaṣṭāḥ kauravā mṛdhe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 124, Verse 30
diṣṭyā vikarṇibhiḥ karṇo raṇe nītaḥ parābhavam vimukhaś ca kṛtaḥ śalyo yuvābhyāṃ puruṣarṣabhau diṣṭyā yuvāṃ kuśalinau saṃgrāmāt punar āgatau paśyāmi rathināṃ śreṣṭhāv ubhau yuddhaviśāradau mama vākyakarau vīrau mama gauravayantritau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 125, Verse 1
durmanā niḥśvasann uṣṇo bhagnadaṃṣṭra ivoragaḥ āgaskṛt sarvalokasya putras te 'rtiṃ parām agāt dṛṣṭvā tat kadanaṃ ghoraṃ svabalasya kṛtaṃ mahat jiṣṇunā bhīmasenena sātvatena ca saṃyuge sa vivarṇaḥ kṛśo dīno bāṣpaviplutalocanaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 125, Verse 6
vadho yena pratijñātaḥ saṃyuge savyasācinaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 126, Verse 4

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 126, Verse 10

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 126, Verse 13

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 126, Verse 17

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 126, Verse 19
tad dhi naḥ krodhavṛkṣaś ca kṛtamūlo mahātmanām tasya puṣpaphale rājann upabhuṃkṣva mahābala

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 126, Verse 39
dīrgham uṣṇaṃ viniḥśvasya kṣatriyāntakaro balī

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 127, Verse 6
pratijñāyā gataḥ pāraṃ hṛtvā saindhavam arjunaḥ paśya rādheya pṛthvīśān pṛthivyāṃ pātitān bahūn pārthena nihatān saṃkhye mahendropamavikramān anicchataḥ kathaṃ vīra droṇasya yudhi pāṇḍavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 127, Verse 10
trāsyāmi saindhavaṃ yuddhe nainaṃ prāpsyati phalgunaḥ mama sainyavināśāya ruddho vipreṇa saindhavaḥ tasya me mandabhāgasya yatamānasya saṃyuge hatāni sarvasainyāni hato rājā jayadrathaḥ paśya yodhavarān karṇa śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ pārthanāmāṅkitair bāṇaiḥ sarve nītā yamakṣayam katham ekarathenājau bahūnāṃ naḥ prapaśyatām vipannaḥ saindhavo rājā yodhāś caiva sahasraśaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 127, Verse 12
yathābalaṃ yathotsāhaṃ tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ yady enaṃ samatikramya praviṣṭaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ nātra sūkṣmo 'pi doṣaḥ syād ācāryasya kathaṃ cana kṛtī dakṣo yuvā śūraḥ kṛtāstro laghuvikramaḥ divyāstrayuktam āsthāya rathaṃ vānaralakṣaṇam kṛṣṇena ca gṛhītāśvam abhedyakavacāvṛtaḥ gāṇḍīvam ajaraṃ divyaṃ dhanur ādāya vīryavān pravarṣan niśitān bāṇān bāhudraviṇadarpitaḥ yad arjuno 'bhyayād droṇam upapannaṃ hi tasya tat ācāryaḥ sthaviro rājañ śīghrayāne tathākṣamaḥ bāhuvyāyāmaceṣṭāyām aśaktas tu narādhipa tenainam abhyatikrāntaḥ śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇasārathiḥ tasmād doṣaṃ na paśyāmi droṇasyānena hetunā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 127, Verse 22
tena yukto hi puruṣaḥ kāryākāryaṃ niyujyate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 128, Verse 25
sā tena pāṇḍavī senā vadhyamānā śilīmukhaiḥ tava putreṇa saṃgrāme vidudrāva narādhipa taṃ tapantam ivādityaṃ kururājaṃ mahāhave nāśakan vīkṣituṃ rājan pāṇḍuputrasya sainikāḥ tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā kupito rājasattama abhyadhāvat kurupatiṃ tava putraṃ jigīṣayā tāv ubhau yudhi kauravyau samīyatur ariṃdamau svārthahetoḥ parākrāntau duryodhanayudhiṣṭhirau tato duryodhanaḥ kruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥ vivyādha daśabhis tūrṇaṃ dhvajaṃ ciccheda ceṣuṇā indrasenaṃ tribhiś caiva lalāṭe jaghnivān nṛpa sārathiṃ dayitaṃ rājñaḥ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ dhanuś ca punar anyena cakartāsya mahārathaḥ caturbhiś caturaś caiva bāṇair vivyādha vājinaḥ tato yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kruddho nimeṣād iva kārmukam anyad ādāya vegena kauravaṃ pratyavārayat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 128, Verse 28
vṛtreṇa saha yudhyantaṃ yadvad devā śatakratum

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 128, Verse 29

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 128, Verse 32
tam evaṃvādinaṃ vīraṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ mahāratham

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 129, Verse 3

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 129, Verse 4
nirdahan sarvasainyāni pāñcālānāṃ ratharṣabhaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 129, Verse 21

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 129, Verse 35
tāni nāgasahasrāṇi rathānām ayutāni ca padātihayasaṃghānāṃ prayutāny arbudāni ca droṇenaikena nārācair nirbhinnāni niśāmukhe

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 130, Verse 9
teṣāṃ saṃloḍyamānānāṃ pāṇḍavair hatacetasām andhe tamasi kiṃ jyotir abhavat kā matis tadā prahṛṣṭāṃś cāpy udagrāṃś ca nityaṃ śaṃsasi pāṇḍavān aprahṛṣṭān vimanaso vitrastāṃś caiva māmakān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 130, Verse 17
tato 'sya sārathiṃ kṣipram anyaṃ duryodhano 'diśat sa tena saṃgṛhītāśvaḥ punar abhyadravad ripūn

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 130, Verse 21
tasmiṃs tathā hate tena siṃhanādo mahān abhūt pāñcālānāṃ mahārāja sādhu sādhv iti pāṇḍavam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 130, Verse 23
yathā kācamaṇir nyasto muṣṭinaikena līlayā sa hataḥ sahasā cūrṇo raktam evopapadyata tathā cūrṇam abhūt tatra karṇabhrātā drumas tathā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 130, Verse 25
pādayor gṛhya tau vīrau bhīmaḥ karṇasya paśyataḥ bhūmāv āvidhya jaghne sa tau ca prāṇair vyayujyatām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 130, Verse 27
etat kṛtvā mahat karma raṇe 'dbhutaparākramaḥ punaḥ svaratham āsthāya dudrāva tava vāhinīm tam āyāntaṃ jighāṃsantaṃ bhīmaṃ kruddham ivāntakam nyavārayan mahābāhuṃ tava putrā viśāṃ pate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 130, Verse 33
āruroha mahābāhur miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvinām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 130, Verse 39
tato yamau drupadasutāḥ sasainikā yudhiṣṭhiradrupadavirāṭasātvatāḥ ghaṭotkaco jayavijayau drumau vṛkaḥ sasṛṃjayās tava tanayān avārayan

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 131, Verse 5
karmaṇas tasya durvṛtta phalaṃ prāpnuhi saṃyuge adya chetsyāmi te mūḍha śiro vikramya patriṇā

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 131, Verse 9
kauraveya na me trāsaḥ kathaṃ cid api vidyate tvayā sārdham athānyaiś ca yudhyato hṛdi kaś cana yadi sarveṇa sainyena gupto māṃ yodhayiṣyasi tathāpi na vyathā kā cit tvayi syān mama kaurava yuddhasāreṇa vākyena satām avamatena ca nāhaṃ bhīṣayituṃ śakyaḥ kṣatravṛtte sthitas tvayā yadi te 'sti yuyutsādya mayā saha narādhipa nirdayo niśitair bāṇaiḥ prahara praharāmi te

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 131, Verse 26
mahāntaṃ ratham āsthāya triṃśan natvāntarāntaram vikṣiptayantrasaṃnāhaṃ mahāmeghaughanisvanam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 131, Verse 30
tatas taṃ giriśṛṅgābhaṃ bhīmarūpaṃ bhayāvaham daṃṣṭrākarālogramukhaṃ śaṅkukarṇaṃ mahāhanum ūrdhvakeśaṃ virūpākṣaṃ dīptāsyaṃ nimnitodaram mahābhrābhagaladvāraṃ kirīṭacchannamūrdhajam trāsanaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakam vīkṣya dīptam ivāyāntaṃ ripuvikṣobhakāriṇam tam udyatamahācāpaṃ rākṣasendraṃ ghaṭotkacam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 131, Verse 39
tato ghaṭotkacaḥ kruddhaś cakraṃ cikṣepa satvaram

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 131, Verse 60

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 131, Verse 107

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 131, Verse 120

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 131, Verse 127

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 132, Verse 4

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 132, Verse 16

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 132, Verse 20

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 134, Verse 1

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 134, Verse 2
yad arjunaguṇāṃs tathyān kīrtayānaṃ narādhama śūradveṣāt sudurbuddhe tvaṃ bhartsayasi mātulam vikatthamānaḥ śauryeṇa sarvalokadhanurbhṛtam darpotsekagṛhīto 'dya na kaṃ cid gaṇayan mṛdhe kva te vīryaṃ kva cāstrāṇi yat tvāṃ nirjitya saṃyuge gāṇḍīvadhanvā hatavān prekṣatas te jayadratham yena sākṣān mahādevo yodhitaḥ samare purā tam icchasi vṛthā jetuṃ sūtādhama manorathaiḥ yaṃ hi kṛṣṇena sahitaṃ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam jetuṃ na śaktāḥ sahitāḥ sendrā api surāsurāḥ lokaikavīram ajitam arjunaṃ sūta saṃyuge kiṃ punas tvaṃ sudurbuddhe sahaibhir vasudhādhipaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 134, Verse 9
duryodhanavacaḥ śrutvā aśvatthāmā mahābalaḥ prasādam agamad rājan sūtaputrasya mānada tataḥ kṛpa uvācedam ācāryaḥ sumahāmanāḥ saumyasvabhāvād rājendra kṣipram āgatamārdavaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 134, Verse 33
bībhatsur api rājendra pāñcālair abhisaṃvṛtaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 134, Verse 40

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 134, Verse 41
tūrṇaṃ jyāṃ ca samāropya gāṇḍīve ca navāṃ dṛḍhām

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 134, Verse 51
sa nunno 'rjunabāṇaughair ācitaḥ śalyako yathā jīvitārtham abhiprepsuḥ kṛpasya ratham āruhat

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 134, Verse 78
aśvatthāmaṃs tvarāyukto yāhi śīghram ariṃdama

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 134, Verse 80
tasmāt tvaṃ puruṣavyāghra pāñcālāñ jahi sānugān

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 134, Verse 81
na tvāṃ samarthāḥ saṃgrāme pāṇḍavāḥ saha somakaiḥ balād yodhayituṃ vīra satyam etad bravīmi te gaccha gaccha mahābāho na naḥ kālātyayo bhavet iyaṃ hi dravate senā pārthasāyakapīḍitā śakto hy asi mahābāho divyena svena tejasā nigrahe pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ pāñcālānāṃ ca mānada

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 135, Verse 1

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 135, Verse 8

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 137, Verse 8

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 137, Verse 43

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 137, Verse 47

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 137, Verse 51

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 138, Verse 13

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 138, Verse 14

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 142, Verse 38

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 143, Verse 20

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 148, Verse 6

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 155, Verse 0
dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ tasmin hate mahāmāye mahātejasi rākṣase amarṣitāḥ pāṇḍaveyāḥ kim akurvan mahāraṇe marditāś ca bhṛśaṃ yuddhe kim akurvata saṃjaya ye ca te 'bhyadravan droṇaṃ vyūḍhānīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ sṛñjayāḥ saha pāñcālais te 'kurvan kiṃ mahāraṇe saumadatter vadhād droṇam āyattaṃ saindhavasya ca amarṣāj jīvitaṃ tyaktvā gāhamānaṃ varūthinīm jṛmbhamāṇam iva vyāghraṃ vyāttānanam ivāntakam kathaṃ pratyudyayur droṇam ajayyaṃ kurusṛñjayāḥ ācāryaṃ ye ca rakṣanti duryodhanapurogamāḥ drauṇikarṇakṛpās tāta te hy akurvan kim āhave bhāradvājaṃ jighāsantau savyasācivṛkodarau ārchatāṃ māmakān yuddhe kathaṃ saṃjaya śaṃsa me sindhurājavadheneme ghaṭotkacavadhena te amarṣitāś ca saṃkruddhā raṇaṃ cakruḥ kathaṃ yudhi

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 157, Verse 17

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 157, Verse 29

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 158, Verse 28

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 158, Verse 29

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 160, Verse 22

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 161, Verse 2

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 161, Verse 17

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 161, Verse 26

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 161, Verse 28

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 161, Verse 33
sa tābhyām ardito vṛddho vṛddhābhyāṃ krodhamūrchitaḥ tau śaraiś chādayām āsa virāṭadrupadāv ubhau droṇena chādyamānau tau kruddhau saṃgrāmamūrdhani droṇaṃ śarair vivyadhatuḥ paramaṃ krodham āsthitau tato droṇo mahārāja krodhāmarṣasamanvitaḥ bhallābhyāṃ bhṛśatīkṣṇābhyāṃ ciccheda dhanuṣī tayoḥ tato virāṭaḥ kupitaḥ samare tomarān daśa daśa cikṣepa ca śarān droṇasya vadhakāṅkṣayā śaktiṃ ca drupado ghorām āyasīṃ svarṇabhūṣitām cikṣepa bhujagendrābhāṃ kruddho droṇarathaṃ prati tato bhallaiḥ suniśitaiś chittvā tāṃs tomarān daśa śaktiṃ kanakavaiḍūryāṃ droṇaś ciccheda sāyakaiḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 161, Verse 46
athodyamya gadāṃ bhīmaḥ kāladaṇḍam ivāntakaḥ droṇāya vyasṛjad rājan rathahayapapalvuve (sic) sāśvasūtadhvajaṃ rājan droṇasyāpothayat tadā prāmṛda[dna]n svabahūn yodhān vāyuvṛkṣān ivaujasā anyaṃ tu ratham āsthāya droṇaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ vyūhadvāraṃ samāsthāya yuddhāya samavasthitaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 162, Verse 4

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 164, Verse 92

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 165, Verse 1

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 165, Verse 61

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 168, Verse 7

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 168, Verse 9
kathaṃ vṛddheṣu tiṣṭhatsu dhārmikeṣu mahatsu ca draupadī prāpnuyāt kleśaṃ veśyā yoṣeva bhārata kim u teṣāṃ bilvaphalaṃ mukhe hy āsīn mahātmanām utāho badhirā hy āsan mūkā vāpi dhanaṃjaya andhā vasaṃs tadā te tu yaiś ca noktaṃ hitaṃ vacaḥ atha tatra bhaved dharmo na caivātrāsty anāryakam anurūpaṃ kṛtaṃ cāpi bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādibhiḥ putraiḥ śiṣyaiś ca yat sārdhaṃ saṃnaddhā yoddhum āhave

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 168, Verse 10

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 168, Verse 30

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 168, Verse 38

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 168, Verse 39
na kṣatriya iti prāhur yo na hanti raṇājire pitaraṃ vā guruṃ vāpi jighāṃsuṃ putraśiṣyayoḥ jihmena vāpy ajihmena hanyād evāvicārayan ity uktaṃ brahmaṇā pūrvaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ dviṣadvadhe tasmāc chiṣyeṇa nihataḥ śatrur me brāhmaṇabruvaḥ yaḥ kṣatriyasuto hanyāt pitaraṃ vā guruṃ ca vā aniṣṭaṃ kṣatriyo hanyāt sa vai kṣatriya ucyate

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 169, Verse 9

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 169, Verse 19

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 169, Verse 23
varaṃ hi te mṛtaṃ pāpa na ca te vṛttam īdṛśam śrotuṃ vaktavyatāmūlaṃ nīcā vakṣyanti mānavāḥ parān kṣipanti doṣeṇa sveṣu doṣeṣv adṛṣṭayaḥ

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 169, Verse 37

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 169, Verse 46

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 169, Verse 60
tau vṛṣāv iva nardantau balinau bāhuśālinau

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 170, Verse 8
bherīś cāvādayan hṛṣṭāḥ paṭahān dundubhīṃś ca ha āḍambarān mṛdaṅgāṃś ca jharjharīś cānakān api maḍḍukān paṇavān vīṇā ḍiṇḍimāṃś ca sahasraśaḥ sarve caiva maheṣvāsā dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān mahāsvanān tato nanāda vasudhā khuranemisamāhatā sa śabdas tumulaḥ khaṃ ca pṛthivīṃ ca vyanādayat kurūṇām atha taṃ śabdaṃ śrutvā ghoraṃ samutthitam pāṇḍavāḥ somakaiḥ sārdhaṃ samapadyanta vismitāḥ te tu dṛṣṭvā kurūn rājan nadato bhairavān ravān abhyavartanta vegena mṛtyuṃ kṛtvā nivartanam

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 170, Verse 13
cukṣubhe pṛthivī sarvā diśaś ca pratisasvanuḥ saṃbhrāntāni ca bhūtāni jalajāny api māriṣa te ca sarve tathā yaudhāḥ saṃprahṛṣṭā yuyutsavaḥ vartamāne tathā śabde raudre tasmin bhayānake saṃpatatsu rathaugheṣu tava teṣāṃ ca bhārata

// Parva 7, Adhyaya 170, Verse 17
